# Resonance Dream IDEAS вЂ” living queue

Each idea has a status (`queued` / `in-progress` / `demoable` / `polished` / `dead`),
a slug (becomes the route `/dream/<n>-<slug>`), and a spec terse enough for
the Dream Agent to build from. Add new ideas to the bottom; promote
items by editing status in place.

The agent appends new ideas here from research cycles. Karel adds ideas
via Claude Code conversation; assistant transcribes into this file.

---

## В§418 banked seeds (cycle 418, KIDS DEEP вЂ” one concept, *the lab's first GAME-CONTROLLER instrument for a 4-year-old, off the glass*, via three interaction approaches on the Gamepad API + dual-rumble haptics; both losers build-complete [clean ESLint + tsc in isolation], `rm -rf`'d after losing to `587-kids-button-garden`; resurrect by re-spawning the brief, renumber on revival вЂ” max committed folder now 587)

- **`586-kids-light-painter`** (status: `queued` В· ~3/5 В· resurrect as an EXPRESSIVE / older-kid or adult controller piece, or as 587's "advanced mode") вЂ” **"What if you PAINTED warm light and bent a chord with two thumbsticks?"** Left + right thumbsticks each pull a continuous additive Canvas2D light-ribbon; stick *magnitude* continuously **bends** a sustained just-intonation A-major-add9 over an A2 root+fifth drone via `setTargetAtTime` portamento (no discrete taps), lowpass opening with deflection; face buttons bloom bell-bursts, triggers swell the drone, dual-rumble pulses with chord motion. Keyboard (WASD/arrows + Z/X/C) + pointer-drag fallbacks + idle Lissajous auto-demo. Tags: gamepad INPUT В· Canvas2D OUTPUT В· continuous-portamento-chord-bend TECH В· warm-expressive VIBE. Refs: Toshio Iwai *Electroplankton*/*TENORI-ON*; May 2026 Steam Controller haptic-song demos. **LOST to 587 (legibility, not quality):** the most *musically expressive* of the three (continuous bend = real warmth), but **two-stick coordination + "push harder = higher" is the least graspable for a 4-year-old** вЂ” it reads as a slightly-adult instrument. **Resurrect** for an adult/older-kid expressive-controller fire, or fold its continuous chord-bend into 587 as a held-trigger "expressive" layer. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (701), `README.md`.

- **`588-kids-glow-drive`** (status: `queued` В· ~3/5 В· resurrect for a calm SPATIAL / exploratory kids fire, or as 587's one-stick younger sibling) вЂ” **"What if you steered a glowing comet through a dark sky and woke sleeping stars that sing as you pass?"** Left stick steers a comet through a fixed autonomous field of light-seeds; the nearest seed wakes/ripples/sings when you pass, pitched by its *place* in the field (a just-intonation spatial scale, low-leftв†’high-right) over a root+fifth drone; right stick blooms a halo, triggers leave a trail + swell, dual-rumble buzzes on each wake. Keyboard/WASD + pointer-drag-to-steer + idle wandering auto-demo. Tags: gamepad INPUT В· Canvas2D OUTPUT В· spatial-scale-field TECH В· calm-exploratory VIBE. Refs: same (Iwai; Steam Controller). **LOST to 587:** lovely and the cleanest answer to the frozen-creature ban (a *field*, not a pet), and one-stick steering is more accessible than 586's two вЂ” but the reward is more **ambient/passive** than 587's instant mashв†’bloom causeв†’effect, and "steer precisely enough to pass near a seed" needs more motor control than a 4-year-old's button-mash. **Resurrect** for a spatial/ambient kids fire, or as the younger-sibling one-stick mode of a controller suite. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (646), `README.md`.

## В§415 banked seeds (cycle 415, ADULT WIDE вЂ” 3 orthogonal explorers all chasing the jury's WARMTH dare; both losers build-complete in isolation, `rm -rf`'d after losing to `580-tide-breath`; resurrect by re-spawning the brief, renumber on revival вЂ” max committed folder now 580)

- **`581-still-bloom`** (status: `queued` В· ~2вЂ“3/5 В· resurrect to open the off-glass / audio-first / conceptual lane the jury keeps naming as 0Г—) вЂ” **"What if music rewarded you for holding completely still?"** An INVERSE gate: a warm ~5вЂ“7-voice just-intonation drone (low root, detuned sine/triangle pairs) slowly BLOOMS out of silence вЂ” voices entering one by one, master lowpass opening 400в†’3500 Hz вЂ” only while you hold the device truly still; any motion above a gentle threshold scatters it (voices duck, bloom recedes). **Off the glass:** input is `DeviceMotion` agitation (rolling variance of acceleration; iOS 13+ `requestPermission()` inside the start gesture), falling back to pointer-stillness, then a guided "breathe-with-me" auto-demo. Audio-FIRST: the visual is a minimal warm Canvas2D radial bloom (NOT three.js/WebGL) that grows with integrated stillness and disperses into grain on motion. Tags: device-motion-stillness INPUT В· audio-first/Canvas2D OUTPUT В· stillness-integration TECH В· warm-meditative/conceptual VIBE. Refs: Pauline Oliveros *Deep Listening*, Г‰liane Radigue, John Cage *4'33"*, Christine Sun Kim. **LOST to 580:** lowest ambition of the trio, does NOT revive the jury-starved WebGPU, and its real payoff needs a held-still device вЂ” at a silent 06:30 glance Karel sees only the breathe-demo, not the felt reward (580 plays autonomously). The strongest pure *concept* and the cleanest answer to the off-glass / audio-only provocation вЂ” resurrect on a cycle where the data/WebGPU lanes are crowded and the lab needs to get off the screen. (No API route; pure client motion + Web Audio, nothing recorded/sent. Build-clean in isolation: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `motion.ts`, `render.ts`, `README.md`.)

- **`582-piano-aurora`** (status: `queued` В· ~2вЂ“3/5 В· resurrect for a "use Karel's real music" fire / a warm WebGPU-painting fire) вЂ” **"What if the *harmony* of a warm piano painted living light?"** A warm piano source (a built-in soft-attack generative IвЂ“viвЂ“IVвЂ“V pad in D with 7ths/9ths so it always plays, PLUS a drop-your-own-recording file input вЂ” the production path being the existing `/api/audio/[id]` route to Karel's Welcome Home tracks, documented not implemented) feeds an `AnalyserNode`; each frame folds the spectrum into a **12-bin chroma** (pitch-class energy, NOT onset/beat) + RMS. The dominant pitch-classes steer the HUE of a **WebGPU curl-noise flow-field aurora** (~40k particles via a WGSL compute pass; Bridson curl noise) confined to a warm amberв†’roseв†’violet arc (cyan/cold-green skipped), RMS drives brightness/flow; hot-downgrades to a ~4k-particle Canvas2D flow field if `navigator.gpu` fails. Tags: audio-file INPUT В· WebGPU OUTPUT (Canvas2D fallback) В· FFT-chroma flow-field TECH В· warm-intimate VIBE. Refs: Refik Anadol (data-painting), Memo Akten (*Learning to See* / flow fields), Robert Bridson (curl noise). **LOST to 580:** it is fundamentally an audio-reactive *visualizer*, and the lab's flow-field/aurora-visualizer lane is crowded (`130-tsl-particle-compute`вќ¤пёЏ, `262-aurora-particle`вќ¤пёЏ, `441-latent-listening-room`) вЂ” close to the jury's standing "renderer flex in search of a concept" critique (its 541 call-out) вЂ” and it carries no real-world data (jury #2). The "harmony-not-rhythm" chroma steering is a genuinely nice twist and it honors the under-served "use his real music" directive вЂ” resurrect by binding it to his ACTUAL Welcome Home tracks via `/api/audio/[id]` (the differentiator that lifts it out of the visualizer pack). (No API route in the prototype itself; dropped audio decoded locally, never uploaded. Build-clean in isolation: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `chroma.ts`, `field.ts`, `gpu.ts`, `README.md`.)

## В§412 banked seeds (cycle 412, KIDS DEEP вЂ” one concept, *today's REAL local weather, played as a kids music window*, via three renderer/interaction approaches on live Open-Meteo; both losers build-complete [clean tsc+eslint], `rm -rf`'d after losing to `575-kids-sky-song`; resurrect by re-spawning the brief, renumber on revival вЂ” max committed folder now 575)

Cycle 412 fired a **kids DEEP** triple off ONE fresh concept вЂ” *open a window onto the child's actual current weather (live Open-Meteo, no key) and play it as music; the live weather composes the key/mood/motion, the child performs within it* вЂ” the directest answer to JURY 2026-06-13 #2 (real-world-data sonification, **0Г— the whole window**) + #4 (chase warmth, not a puzzle), and a grep-verified **kids-first real-data sonification** (the lab's prior weather toys `115`/`120`/`83` are all *synthetic*/"Zero API"; the only real-data pieces `355`/`337` are adult + out of frame). All three share: direct client-side fetch of `api.open-meteo.com` (public, no-key, CORS, **no api route, no guard, no secret**; CSP-verified вЂ” enforced `connect-src вЂ¦ https:` allows it), optional geolocation with a silent default-coordinate fallback (no kids permission gate), a baked demo-sky for offline/failure so the 06:30 glance always shows + plays, WMO `weather_code`+`cloud_cover`+`is_day`в†’consonant-scale/mood mapping, kids-safe `gainв†’lowpass(в‰¤8k)в†’compressorв†’destination` limiter, alive-from-frame-one visuals. Winner shipped = `575-kids-sky-song` (the *generative-composition* take вЂ” the weather writes an evolving look-ahead song that plays itself; the biggest concept + best "reads as music at a silent glance" + most differentiated from the lab's existing synthetic-weather Canvas2D toys). Both losers below are complete, build-reviewed real implementations (own folder, pure client-side, no API route, brick-wall limiter, hands-free auto-demo + baked-sky fallback, graceful WebGL2в†’Canvas2D / geo-denied fallbacks); folders removed per the no-half-built-folders rule, banked here as ready-to-resurrect TEXT.

- **`573-kids-sky-window`** (`queued`, the most *immersive renderer* take вЂ” RESURRECT for a shader-forward weather/atmosphere fire, or as 575's richer sky layer) вЂ” a fullscreen **raw-WebGL2 hand-written-GLSL** living-sky window: fbm volumetric-ish clouds (density from `cloud_cover`), wind-driven drift (`wind_speed/direction`), sun/moon glow+halo (`is_day`+clear), procedural rain streaks / snowflakes (from `precipitation`), night stars, storm lightning, touch ripples/bloom, window vignette вЂ” alive from frame one, with a Canvas2D fallback sky that still shows weather + sings. Touch = play notes quantised to today's weather-set scale (7 moods: sunny major-pentatonic / starry-night octave-down / cloudy sus2 / fog low-drone / rain minor-pentatonic / snow high-bells / storm lydian); `temperature`в†’timbre+register, `wind`в†’drift+filter LFO, `precipitation`в†’falling-voice density. **LOST, not on quality:** the most beautiful sky of the three, but 575's generative engine is the bigger *concept* leap ("the weather *composes*" vs "the weather *tints* what you tap"), and an abstract shader sky reads less instantly than 575's self-blooming notes at a silent glance. **Its value:** the richest atmosphere renderer вЂ” resurrect for an atmosphere/aurora-forward fire, or fold its volumetric sky in as 575's background. Ambition 3/5 (#1 qualified kids-first real-data sonification + #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems + #3 Polli/Miebach/WeatherChimes; #5 not claimed). Complete: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts` (`SkyAudio`), `weather.ts`, `render.ts`, `README.md`. Clean tsc+eslint, not browser-verified.

- **`574-kids-weather-today`** (`queued`, the warmest / most 4yo-legible take) вЂ” a cozy **Canvas2D cut-paper diorama**: paper hills, a smiling sun or moon, drifting clouds, falling rain/snow, and a friendly breathing paper critter вЂ” the most instantly-readable "today's weather" for a 4-year-old. Tap the sun/clouds/critter/hill (each a different position in today's key) в†’ always-consonant music-box notes; scene + key/mode chosen by live `weather_code`+`cloud_cover`+`is_day` (sunny major meadow / overcast sus2 grey hills / rain minor-pentatonic chimes / snow glassy bells / fog hush / thunder weighty minor / starry night), `temperature`в†’color temp + timbre, `wind`в†’cloud drift, `precipitation`в†’particle count; always-on ambient chord bed; tap targets в‰Ґ80px. **LOST:** despite the real-data headline it is the closest in *form* to the lab's existing synthetic weather toys (`115-kids-weather-music` zone-blend, `120-kids-rain-drum` cloud-tap) вЂ” the "too similar in shape" risk вЂ” and the least ambitious renderer of the three (Canvas2D vs WebGL2 + a generative engine). **Its value:** the warmest, coziest, most-legible-to-a-4yo + the most iPad-bulletproof (Canvas2D) вЂ” resurrect when a warmth-forward / maximally-legible kids weather fire is due, or ship it as 575's more-literal sibling for the youngest users. Ambition 3/5 (#1 qualified kids-first real-data sonification + #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems + #3 Polli/Miebach/WeatherChimes; #5 not claimed). Complete: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `weather.ts`, `scene.ts`, `README.md`. Clean tsc+eslint, not browser-verified.

## В§410 banked seeds (cycle 410, KIDS DEEP вЂ” one concept, *a creature genuinely different each day you return*, via what evolves; both losers build-complete, `rm -rf`'d after losing to `569-kids-ember-keeper`; resurrect by re-spawning the brief, renumber on revival вЂ” max committed folder now 569. NOTE: the В§409 banked seeds named `569-conductor-batons`/`570-conductor-baton-motion` are stale number-labels вЂ” those slugs are now taken by this cycle's Ember pieces; renumber the conductor seeds on revival.)

Cycle 410 fired a **kids DEEP** triple off ONE massively-bigger concept вЂ” *a creature that lives in the device, remembers every visit, and is genuinely different each day you return; it never resets* вЂ” attacked via three things that can evolve across days (BODY / SONG / WORLD), all sharing the lab-first **cross-session `localStorage` persistence** + day-aware growth + analysis-only mic-feeding + kids-safe limiter + a fresh-device demo seed + a рџЊ™ next-day time-travel button (so the cross-day payoff reads in <30s at the 06:30 review). Winner shipped = `569-kids-ember-keeper` (the *body-morphology* take вЂ” the most literal answer to JURY #6 "a creature genuinely changed tomorrow", the most glance-legible [you SEE it grew], and the freshest vs the existing kids set). Both losers below are complete, build-reviewed real implementations (own folder, pure client-side, no API route, brick-wall limiter, hands-free seed/auto-demo, graceful mic-denied fallback, no-Canvas2D fallback); folders removed per the no-half-built-folders rule, banked here as ready-to-resurrect TEXT.

- **`570-kids-ember-song`** (`queued`, the biggest *concept* of the trio вЂ” RESURRECT for a music-forward / non-glance-only fire) вЂ” a child's creature **remembers every melody they ever hummed** and, each day they return, sings back a LONGER, RICHER song woven from everything taught вЂ” never the same twice, never reset. Hummed phrases (autocorrelation pitch в†’ pentatonic snap в†’ silence-segmented into a phrase of scale-degrees + coarse rhythm, `pitch.ts`) are **appended forever** to a `localStorage` library (`song-memory.ts`, key `resonance.ember-song.v1`); a tiny seeded **generative weaver** (`weave.ts`, Eno *Music for Airports* lineage) recombines the library each visit, sizing the piece to distinct-days returned (growth 1 = one looped phrase; 3+ = several phrases + an octave-down counter-voice; 4+ = a fuller pad bed). Each remembered phrase = one **luminous orbiting strand** in a raw-**WebGL2** creature (`render.ts`, `MAX_STRANDS` 24) that flares when its notes sound. Look-ahead scheduler (25 ms pump, `start(t)` 120 ms ahead) keeps the weave tight; kids-safe limiter; fresh-device seed = 4 phrases across 4 days. **LOST, not on quality:** the cross-day payoff is *audible* (a longer song), so at a SILENT 06:30 glance the abstract strands read less clearly than 569's visibly-bigger body, and the рџЊ™ button's reward is a thing you must hear. **Its value:** no lab piece grows the *music itself* across sessions вЂ” it's the strongest return-reward concept; ship it when a music-forward kids fire is due (or as 569's cycle-2 "it also sings your grown song"). Ambition 4/5 (#1 cross-session persistence [shared lab-first] + #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems + #3 Eno/Tamagotchi/Oliveros + #4 Ember spine). Complete: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `pitch.ts`, `render.ts`, `song-memory.ts`, `weave.ts`, `README.md`. Build-reviewed, not browser-verified.

- **`571-kids-ember-nest`** (`queued`, the warmest/most-legible take) вЂ” the creature lives in a little **NEST/WORLD that fills up across days**: every visit leaves a permanent **cut-paper flower / star / friend** (matte inline-**SVG** via `feTurbulence`+`feDropShadow`, rAF-via-refs вЂ” no per-frame React churn), and each object is also one **sustained C-pentatonic voice**, so a fuller world is literally a fuller, warmer (always-consonant) **additive chord** (per-voice gain `0.16/в€љn` keeps the sum kids-safe while the texture thickens вЂ” the Eno density move). Day-aware: first wake of a new calendar day auto-sprouts one new permanent object; humming/tapping plants smaller flowers. `localStorage` key `resonance.ember-nest.v1`; fresh-device seed = 9 objects across 4 days with `lastVisitDay` = yesterday; рџЊ™ next-day button thickens the chord on demand. **LOST:** the accumulating-world framing is thematically **closest to the existing `116-kids-bloom-garden`** (self-seeding singing garden) and a glowing-pond/firefly lineage вЂ” the "too similar" risk; and another SVG output nudges the rolling-10 SVG count toward the 4Г— ban (it sat at 3Г—). **Its value:** the warmest, most-immediately-legible-to-a-4yo of the three (a busy nest reads instantly), removes Tamagotchi's punishment/death loop (returning is *always* rewarded, never guilt вЂ” a deliberate kindness), and the additive-chord-from-world-density is lovely; resurrect when SVG is clear and pair it with a non-overlapping placement pass + a voice cap for months-old worlds. Ambition 4/5 (#1 cross-session persistence [shared lab-first] + #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems + #3 Tamagotchi/Reggio Emilia "revisiting"/Eno + #4 Ember spine). Complete: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `pitch.ts`, `scene.ts`, `shapes.ts`, `README.md`. Build-reviewed, not browser-verified.

## В§408 banked seeds (cycle 408, KIDS WIDE вЂ” 3 orthogonal off-glass explorers; both losers build-complete, `rm -rf`'d after losing to `566-kids-shake-band`; resurrect by re-spawning the brief, renumber on revival вЂ” max folder now 566)

Cycle 408 fired a WIDE kids triple off three orthogonal **off-glass** inputs (mic-sing / device-shake / camera-color) Г— non-banned renderers (WebGL2 / three.js / WebGL2), all dodging the rolling-10 **SVG-output ban (4Г—)** and every standing jury ban. Winner shipped = `566-kids-shake-band` (device-motion в†’ three.js batucada band вЂ” the freshest off-glass input vs recent kids cycles + the directest "break the calm-sensory autopilot" answer, and ideal for Karel's mobile review since he can literally shake his phone). Both losers below are complete, build-reviewed real implementations (own folder, pure client-side, no API route, brick-wall limiter, hands-free auto-demo, graceful sensor-denied fallback); folders removed per the no-half-built-folders rule, banked here as ready-to-resurrect TEXT.

- **`565-kids-sing-choir`** (`queued`, the biggest *concept* of the trio вЂ” RESURRECT when a non-mic kids cycle is due) вЂ” a 4-year-old sings/hums one steady note and **four glowing creature-friends instantly join in live harmony** (major 3rd / perfect 5th / octave), the whole choir gliding with the child's pitch in real time вЂ” the child *becomes* the lead of a four-voice chord. Implements **Jacob Collier's live vocal-harmonizer** honestly: detected pitch (YIN-style parabolic-interpolated autocorrelation, RMS-gated, `pitch.ts`) в†’ C-pentatonic snap в†’ 4 detuned-oscillator+vibrato voices tracking via `setTargetAtTime` 40ms glides (`audio.ts`), rendered as raw-WebGL2 additive particle creatures (`page.tsx`, ~746 lines, Canvas2D fallback). **LOST on the diversity gate, not quality:** its input is **mic**, exactly what the *immediately prior* kids cycle (406 clap-canon) used вЂ” repeating the previous kids cycle's primary modality is the "too similar" trap. Also the riskiest unverified surface (pitch detection on a breathy 4yo soprano in a noisy room; it flags wanting a 3вЂ“5-frame median smoother + higher RMS gate). Distinct from the adult `114-live-harmonize` (piano-roll viz) and from `280-echo-canyon`/`179-voice-monster` (those echo *sequentially*, this harmonizes *simultaneously*). **Its value:** no kids piece does live simultaneous vocal harmony вЂ” ship it the next time the diversity audit clears mic. Ambition 3/5 (#2 5 subsystems + #3 Collier; #1 not clean вЂ” live-harmonize exists). Complete: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `pitch.ts`, `README.md`. Build-reviewed, not browser-verified.

- **`567-kids-color-garden`** (`queued`, the off-the-couch explorer) вЂ” point the tablet's **rear camera** at anything colorful in the real world and that color **grows a singing plant** in a glowing WebGL2 garden; warm reds = low notes, cool violets = high, every color welcome, no goal. Implements **Scriabin's *clavier Г  lumiГЁres*** hueв†’pitch map (redв†’C3 вЂ¦ violetв†’D5) honestly. Subsystems: `getUserMedia(environment)` в†’ offscreen-2D central-patch `getImageData` в†’ RGBв†’HSV with 20В°/24-frame **hysteresis** (`vision.ts`), Scriabin hueв†’C-pentatonic map + brick-wall-limited synth + always-on C2+G2 pad (`audio.ts`), instanced additive WebGL2 plants growing rootв†’bloom over ~1.5s with in-shader hsv2rgb (`render.ts`, ~392 lines), hue-cycling auto-demo for the camera-denied path. **LOST:** camera-color is thematically adjacent to the existing `368-kids-rainbow-quest` (foraging quest) and camera is the jury-flagged trodden input lane; it is also the most **lighting-fragile** for the 06:30 hands-free glance (low light / fluorescent flicker destabilize the patch average). **Its value:** the *open-creation* (vs quest) framing + the world-becomes-music exploration is genuinely lovely; resurrect when the camera lane is clear and pair with a more robust dominant-color extractor (k-means / saturation-weighted, not a flat average). Ambition 3/5 (#2 5+ subsystems + #3 Scriabin; #1 not clean вЂ” color-foraging exists at 368). Complete: `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `vision.ts`, `render.ts`, `README.md`. Build-reviewed, not browser-verified.

## В§407 banked seeds (cycle 407, ADULT DEEP вЂ” splat spine cycle 2; both build-complete, `rm -rf`'d after losing to `564-piano-splat-cathedral`; resurrect by re-spawning the brief)

- **`563-piano-splat-ewa`** (`queued`, the reconstruction-grade renderer вЂ” RESURRECT for cycle 3) вЂ” the lab's most technically honest Gaussian-splat renderer: **full EWA covariance projection** (per-splat 3D covariance ОЈ = RВ·diag(s)В·вЂ¦В·RбµЂ from a quaternion; analytic perspective Jacobian J; ОЈ' = TОЈTбµЂ; 2Г—2 conic inversion; eigenvalue-bounded quad) with **premultiplied alpha-over** + per-frame back-to-front depth sort, driven by Karel's real piano (audio.ts + synth fallback). It LOST to 564 only because the *experience* is another orbitable glowing cloud (adjacent to 557's galaxy), where 564 is a categorically new experience (a building his music raises). **Its value:** the true-EWA math is the cleanest #1-technique in the splat spine вЂ” the obvious **cycle-3 move is to swap 564's simplified two-axis anisotropy for 563's full covariance projection** в†’ a reconstruction-grade cathedral. Complete files existed: `page.tsx` (idle demo + Begin), `splat-renderer.ts` (~28kB, all math hand-rolled: quatToMat3 / computeCovariance3D / projectCovariance / invertConic / gaussianRadius), `audio.ts`, `README.md`. Build-reviewed, not browser-verified (numerical fragility on degenerate/off-axis conics is the main risk; it added a 0.3px low-pass regularizer).

- **`562-piano-splat-aurora`** (`queued`, the ribbon/sheet renderer) вЂ” anisotropic splats stretched into flowing **aurora ribbons** (each splat carries a 3D principal axis в†’ screen-space rotation Оё + (ПѓMajor,ПѓMinor); bright/treble notes = thin sharp ribbons, dark/bass = fat puffs), depth-sorted alpha-over with a small additive emissive core for luminosity (Anadol teal/magenta/violet palette). LOST: also a "cloud you orbit," conceptually adjacent to 557. **Its value:** the *anisotropy-from-velocity-tangent* trick (splats elongate along the audio-driven flow) is a clean, cheap way to make sorted splats read as silky sheets вЂ” fold into any future splat piece that wants ribbons over puffs. Complete: `page.tsx`, `splat.ts` (~22kB), `audio.ts`, `README.md`. Build-reviewed, not browser-verified.

### Banked В§406 (WIDE **kids** non-winners вЂ” TEXT seeds, folders removed; renumber on revival, max folder now 559):
Cycle 406 fired a WIDE kids triple off three orthogonal **off-glass** inputs (mic / camera / shake) Г— three different renderers (SVG / three.js / Canvas2D), all dodging the rolling-10 finger-on-glass ban. Winner shipped = `559-kids-clap-canon` (micв†’SVG, Steve Reich phasing вЂ” the jury #4 "time-tension piece, but for children" answer). Both losers below are complete, build-reviewed real implementations (own folder, pure client-side, no API route, brick-wall limiter, hands-free auto-demo, graceful sensor-denied fallback); folders removed per the no-half-built-folders rule, banked here as ready-to-resurrect TEXT.

- **`560-kids-shadow-band`** (camera silhouette, NO ML в†’ three.js particle creature в†’ zone-gated pentatonic band) вЂ” `queued`. **What if a 4-year-old's SHADOW became a glowing creature, and dancing through the air played a band вЂ” no controller, no reading, just their silhouette of light?** INPUT camera frame-differencing (no MediaPipe/TF вЂ” `getUserMedia`в†’96Г—72 offscreen canvasв†’24Г—18 motion-energy grid vs captured background + prev frame, IIR-smoothed) В· OUTPUT **three.js** ~4,096 additive THREE.Points blending toward active grid cells (a luminous "moving aura," not a sharp outline вЂ” correct for frame-diff) В· TECHNIQUE optical-motion-energyв†’3 vertical instrument zones (left bells / center warm-pad / right marimba, rate-limited, motionв†’gain+brightness) В· VIBE embodied/awe/your-body-becomes-light. Master `gainв†’lowpass8kв†’DynamicsCompressor(в€’10/20:1)`; synthetic Lissajous-blob auto-demo runs with zero permission, hands off to real camera, resumes after 4 s still; `text-rose-300` camera-denied + pointer fallback. ## SPINE: Xenharmonic Drone (started Cycle 403 вЂ” the jury 2026-06-12's named 4/5 chase: "538 capped at 3 only because it's a one-off вЂ” make it a spine and it's the first 4")
**The thread:** *the just-intonation / BohlenвЂ“Pierce harmonic lattice stops being something you TAP and becomes a living place вЂ” a self-drifting La Monte Young "Dream House" drone that wanders the Tonnetz via the comma pump and never returns home.* Extends `538-xenharmonic-lattice` (cycle 1, a static SVG Tonnetz you click). **Cycle 2 (403, SHIPPED):** `552-dream-house` вЂ” a fully **autonomous long-form (>5 min, ~14-min arc) generative drone pilgrimage**: a walker steps the lattice every 4вЂ“8 s biased to unvisited nodes, sustaining the nearest 2вЂ“6 nodes as a slow-crossfading pure-ratio chord; an 8-phase arc (gatheringв†’ascendingв†’floweringв†’tritaveв†’radianceв†’dissolvingв†’recedingв†’stillness) drives density (2в†”6 voices), a drifting master lowpass (700в†”4800 Hz), a В±0.4-octave register breath, and a 4-stop tuning migration (5-JIв†’BвЂ“Pв†’19-EDOв†’back); the syntonic comma (81/80) guarantees the pitch never recloses; SVG Tonnetz with a glowing comet-trail + accumulating visited-ghost dots makes the journey visible; HUD shows elapsed/phase. Zero permission, runs itself (ideal 06:30 glance); tap = optional "exhale" to bloom a fresh region. Master `gain в†’ drifting lowpass в†’ DynamicsCompressor(20:1, в€’10 dBFS) в†’ destination`; per-voice gain `0.55/voiceCount`, 8-voice hard cap. Ambition **3/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems [walker + crossfading drone synth + long-form arc engine + SVG render = 4] + #3 named refs [La Monte Young & Zazeela *Dream House* / Г‰liane Radigue / Euler Tonnetz / BohlenвЂ“Pierce / Partch / syntonic comma] + #4 spine cycle 2 вЂ” the jury's exact ask). **#1 the contestable case** вЂ” *first deliberate long-form (>5min) stateful evolving piece* is a counts-as-#1 in the manual, but 514/526 are arguably already long-form autonomous, so it discounts to 3/5 honestly. **#5 NOT claimed** вЂ” arxiv cs.SD June 5вЂ“12 2026 had zero JI/microtonal/pitch papers (still server-ML); said plainly. **No API route** (pure client Web Audio + SVG; no mic/camera/network/secrets). **Cycle 3 (planned):** fold in the banked steering layers below so the pilgrimage is *steerable but still autonomous by default* (grab-the-wheel), and/or bind a genuinely <14-day xenharmonic/JI finding for the long-missing #5.

## SPINE: The Resonant Room (started Cycle 377 вЂ” the adult #4 spine; explored across temperatures)
**The thread:** *a sympathetic resonant room вЂ” an instrument played INTO a tuned acoustic space that rings back вЂ” explored from warm to cold.* **Cycle 1 (377, SHIPPED):** `475-resonant-room` вЂ” Karel's *Welcome Home* piano into a **key-tuned N=8 Householder-matrix Feedback Delay Network** (Jot / StautnerвЂ“Puckette) that rings IN KEY and **resolves to the tonic on release** (the warm partner). **Cycle 2 (379, SHIPPED):** `483-two-rooms-apart` вЂ” the *opposite temperature*: a **live-MIDI**-played room split into **two coupled resonator banks tuned a tritone apart** that beat against each other (no tonic, suspended dissonance), with a **real-time PlompвЂ“Levelt/Sethares roughness** readout; **resolution is the player's act** вЂ” drag detuneв†’unison and the beating fuses. Ambition **4/5** (#1 first-Web-MIDI-INPUT + #2 + #3 + #4; #5 not claimed вЂ” refs foundational). Won a DEEP 3-way fire; the jury (2026-06-10) explicitly asked to *deepen a spine* (not grab a 5th DSP primitive) вЂ” this is an *extension*, one room в†’ two. **Cycle 3 (381, SHIPPED):** `486-third-room` вЂ” adds a THIRD room a **just-fifth (702 Вў = 3:2)** above Room A (its partials lock onto A's, so Aв†”C is consonant) as a **bridge**: blend C in, find the **pivot note** where all three rooms momentarily agree, then collapse the tritone вЂ” *negotiate* the dissonance to rest rather than just collapsing it. Folds in BOTH banked cycle-3 ideas at once вЂ” the **steepest-descent pivot-note suggestion engine** (from `481`, glows the notes that most lower three-room roughness) AND the **WebGPU compute vorticity field** (from `482`, the starved renderer; roughness в†’ per-room vorticity, Canvas2D fallback) вЂ” plus the new third-room mechanic (implements `483`'s own documented cycle-3 idea). Ambition **4/5** (#2 5 subsystems + #3 refs + #4 spine cycle 3 вЂ” the truest *extension*: oneв†’twoв†’three rooms; #1/#5 honestly not claimed). Hits jury (2026-06-10) #1 (tension resolved *through action*) + #2 (deepen, don't grab a primitive) + #3 (ban three.js, pick the starved WebGPU). Won a DEEP 3-way fire (resolution-mechanic axis). **Cycle 4 (planned, pre-scoped from this fire's banked siblings):** (a) port `485`'s **whisper panel** вЂ” a fixed "Notes that ease the tension в†’" list with predicted %-improvement + a derived gradient arrow on the detune slider (the most legible 06:30 read); (b) add `487`'s **roughness landscape + shared-control "descend toward rest" autopilot** as a second resolution axis (feel the slope of the tritoneв†’fifth negotiation; keep it opt-in/overridable so it never becomes a pre-baked release). **No API route** вЂ” pure client-side Web Audio + Web MIDI + WebGPU/Canvas2D; no secrets.

### `464-helios-aurora` вЂ” NOAA **space-weather** (live solar wind + Kp planetary index) в†’ an evolving aurora drone with an **EDM build-and-drop** arc keyed to geomagnetic storms (Kpв‰Ґ5 = the drop, resolving warm). `<audio crossOrigin="anonymous">` (default `/api/audio/549fc519вЂ¦`, or file-drop, or 12-TET synth fallback that resolves) в†’ `createMediaElementSource` в†’ AnalyserNode в†’ lowpassв†’shimmerв†’reverbв†’compressorв†’master. Every ~6.5 s: centroidв†’palette / energyв†’density / pitch-classв†’hue over the Anadol base style в†’ guarded FAL `flux/schnell` (в‰¤1 in flight, в‰Ґ7 s apart) в†’ ~2.5 s cross-fade + Ken-Burns + vignette. Loop-back: 8Г—6 `getImageData` avg color в†’ brightness opens lowpass + shimmer, warmth lengthens reverb вЂ” on the real playback. CORS-taint guard: analyser all-zero >2.5 s в†’ auto-swap to synth + amber status. Built files: `page.tsx` (728), `audio.ts` (458), `field.ts` (259), guarded `api/route.ts`. Refs: Anadol *Unsupervised*/*Machine Hallucinations* В· Akten *Learning to See*. Ambition: #4 (spine cycle-1 alt) + #2 (в‰Ґ3 subsystems) + #3 (named refs). **Why it lost:** it is the *least differentiated from `441`* вЂ” re-presents the existing mechanic on a new source, which the jury explicitly penalizes вЂ” though it is the safest hands-free read. **Why resurrect:** the cleanest, most reliable spine foundation; ship it if a cycle wants the rock-solid real-audio loop with no analysis risk. **Next-cycle deepening:** it IS the spine's stable base вЂ” layer the cycle-2 multi-agent captioning onto this if `448`'s onset-timed regeneration proves too eager/sparse on real piano.

### `449-piano-latent-grains` вЂ” the AGGRESSIVE loop-back: the dreamed image RE-COMPOSES the piano as granular re-synthesis *(banked sibling вЂ” the strongest cycle-3 deepening candidate)*
A `GranularEngine` schedules Hann-windowed grains (в‰¤24 voices в†’ DynamicsCompressor) off the **decoded** piano buffer (default `/api/audio/549fc519вЂ¦` в†’ fetch signed URL в†’ `decodeAudioData`; or file-drop; or an `OfflineAudioContext`-rendered Cв†’Amв†’Fв†’Gв†’C resolving phrase). The image *re-composes the grains*: **brightness в†’ grain density + read-head scatter**, **warmth в†’ pitch-spread (В±semitones) + reverb wet**, **texture/variance в†’ grain-duration jitter** вЂ” so a bright busy image scatters the piano into a shimmering detuned cloud, a dark calm image lets it settle back toward the original. AnalyserNode on the grain output drives the ~6 s prompt; full-bleed canvas cross-fades the FAL image with grain motes (pitch-class-colored) drifting over it, or a local latent field when no key. Built files: `page.tsx` (916), `granular.ts` (334), guarded `api/route.ts`. Refs: Curtis Roads *Microsound* (2001) В· Anadol *Machine Hallucinations* В· rides loved `227-paths-granular`вќ¤пёЏ + `323-latent-condensation`вќ¤пёЏ. Ambition: #4 (spine cycle-1 alt) + #2 + #3. **Why it lost:** graining a *real* recording is the highest browser-verification risk (mush/artifact danger) for a build-only sandbox вЂ” but on pure surprise it was the closest contender. **Why resurrect:** it is the literal answer to the spine's cycle-3 goal вЂ” the image *reshapes* the music, not just filters it; fold its granular loop-back into the spine once `448`'s base is browser-verified. **Next-cycle deepening:** add a transient-preserving grain mode so attacks survive, and let onset/phrase detection (from `448`) gate grain bursts to musical events.

### `445-kids-light-river` вЂ” paint a glowing, singing river of light with ANY whole-body motion вЂ” no model, no WebGPU, the most robust take *(banked sibling вЂ” the resilient maximum-06:30-reliability ship)*

### `430-wiki-pulse` вЂ” the LIVE Wikimedia recent-changes firehose sonified: every edit on Earth, right now, bots vs humans *(banked sibling вЂ” the real-world-data + "music about something other than music" take; the freshest data SOURCE the lab has)*
- **Tags** (clean dodge of all bans): INPUT = **external SSE data** (Wikimedia EventStreams, public/keyless/CORS, client-side `EventSource` вЂ” NO api route, no guard) В· OUTPUT = **three.js** (rising glowing nodes, additive bloom) В· TECHNIQUE = real-time event-stream sonification В· VIBE = restless/global/never-resolving.
- **The mechanic:** connects to `https://stream.wikimedia.org/v2/stream/recentchange`, keeps `type==="edit"||"new"`, reads `wiki`/`bot`/`user`/`length.{old,new}` в†’ `delta`. **delta** (log-scaled) drives amplitude/duration/base-freq (big additions bloom deep & swelling, tiny edits soft high ticks; sign changes timbre вЂ” deletions glide down with a gritty high-passed breath); **bot vs human в†’ two distinct timbres** (bots dry/mechanical/quantized square blips; humans warm/breathy/resonant triangle-through-moving-LPF + noise breath вЂ” "you can hear the machines vs the people," the emotional core); **wiki/language в†’ stereo pan** (westв†’east spread + micro-detune); always-on detuned-sine bed; master `DynamicsCompressor` brick-wall limiter + voice cap. Each edit also spawns a rising three.js sphere (size = log|delta|, humans warm / bots cool, x = pan). **Reliability:** a single Begin gesture creates/resumes the AudioContext (iOS); a **deterministic seeded synthetic firehose** drives the EXACT same pipeline if no live event arrives within ~2.5s (amber "offline demo" notice в†’ green "в—Џ live" when real events flow), so it always comes alive hands-free in ~2s. Built files: `page.tsx` (~670), `README.md`. **Refs:** **Hatnote *Listen to Wikipedia*** (LaPorte & Hashemi, 2013 вЂ” the canonical Wikipedia-edit sonification; this is a darker, non-consonant, three.js take) + **Wikimedia EventStreams**.
- **Why it didn't win:** the highest-*concept* surprise of the slate and the most direct answer to the jury's #4 ("zero real-world-data sonification in 15 cycles вЂ” sonify an external API, it breaks the mic rut AND the consonance rut in one fire"), BUT data-sonification is **explicitly NOT a lab-first** (`314-solar-wind` / `337`/`418-seismic` already did it вЂ” corrected IDEAS В§359), so it tops out at **ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3-subsystems: EventSource ingest + Web-Audio synth + three.js render В· #3 named-ref) where `432` clears 3/5 with a grep-verified #1. **Revive:** the obvious next **real-world-data ship** вЂ” it's the freshest data SOURCE the lab has (not seismic/solar) and breaks the mic+consonance ruts together; **fix-first:** add per-region timbre color (currently language is pan-only) and orchestrate dense bursts instead of thinning at the voice cap. Reconstructable from this spec.

### `431-test-signal` вЂ” clinical Ikeda / Alva-Noto GLITCH-WALL instrument, raw-WebGL2 data-card *(banked sibling вЂ” the purest clinical refuse-to-resolve swing; jury #2)*
- **Tags:** INPUT = **keyboard/touch** (toggle + sculpt channels) В· OUTPUT = **raw WebGL2** (hand-written GLSL monochrome test-card) В· TECHNIQUE = sine-sweep + look-ahead impulse-grid + bit-crush glitch (no scale) В· VIBE = clinical/abrasive/unresolved.
- **The mechanic:** three independent signal channels, nothing pitched to a scale. **SWEEP** (key 1) вЂ” a continuous log-glide sine (top capped 9 kHz, amplitude rolled off as freq climbs) + gliding sub. **IMPULSE** (key 2) вЂ” band-passed filtered-noise clicks scheduled with a Web-Audio **look-ahead scheduler** (Chris Wilson "Two Clocks", 25ms tick / 100ms ahead), `RATE`/`DENS` controls, no pitch. **GLITCH** (key 3) вЂ” bit-crush via quantizing `WaveShaperNode` + sample-hold playbackRate + stutter gate, `RATE`/`BRGHT`. All в†’ master gain в†’ brick-wall `DynamicsCompressor` (в€’6 dB / ratio 20) в†’ analyser в†’ out. Raw-WebGL2 GLSL data-card: sweep-tracking scan line, density-shifting barcode field, impulse-strobed columns (localized + soft, **no full-screen strobe**), glitch displacement/block-noise, a live oscilloscope trace of the master output; `prefers-reduced-motion` в†’ `u_calm` dampens everything. **Reliability:** Begin creates/resumes the ctx in-gesture (iOS), then auto-sequences SWEEPв†’IMPULSEв†’GLITCH (~0.3/2.1/4.2s) hands-free, then fully interactive (cards в‰Ґ44px + keys). Built files: `page.tsx` (~841), `README.md`. **Refs:** **Ryoji Ikeda** (*test pattern* / *dataplex* / *data.matrix*) + **Alva Noto / Carsten Nicolai** (*Xerrox*, clicks-and-glitch).
- **Why it didn't win:** a genuine, safety-serious commitment to the Ikeda/Alva-Noto idiom (un-snapped glide, real look-ahead scheduler, dependency-free bit-crush, GLSL data-card driven by live audio state) вЂ” but **ambition 2/5** (#2 + #3; refuse-to-resolve is the *framing*, not a novel technique) and the lab already swung at refuse-to-resolve twice recently (`357-shatter`, `422`), so it's the second piece at the same mandate rather than a new capability. **Revive:** ship next time the adult lane wants the *pure clinical* register on its own renderer (raw-WebGL2, distinct from 357's DOM/CSS and 422's grid); **deepen-first:** make the impulse grid a programmable pattern sequencer and the glitch channel player-triggerable as discrete one-shots (both self-flagged) to push it from "ambient generator" to "instrument." Reconstructable from this spec.

## Banked from Cycle 360 (DEEP kids fire вЂ” *finger-paint where the brush's TEXTURE is its SOUND, noise not notes*. Both siblings are complete, **build-reviewed** real implementations (~900вЂ“1300 lines, folder-isolated, ESLint-discipline followed); folders removed per the no-half-built-folders rule, banked here as ready-to-resurrect TEXT. Shared thesis: every kids sound toy maps to pentatonic PITCH; these make the whole palette NOISE/TIMBRE. **Renderer note for revival: Canvas2D is now 4Г— in the trailing window в†’ 428 (WebGL2) is the cleaner lane; renumber on revival, max folder now 429.**)

### `428-kids-texture-paint-morph` вЂ” subtractive noise-morph on a raw-WebGL2 painterly canvas *(banked sibling вЂ” the BEAUTIFUL take + the obvious cycle-2 deepening)*
- **Concept:** same toy as 429 (paint a texture, hear it) but the sound is **continuous subtractive synthesis** вЂ” an always-running noise bed (white + brown) sculpted live by resonant biquad filters: finger X в†’ filter centre/brightness, Y в†’ Q/resonance, drag-speed в†’ energy. Textures: рџЊ¬пёЏ Wind (bandpass-swept brown noise) В· рџ’§ Water (resonant bubbling) В· рџЏњпёЏ Sand (narrow high hiss) В· рџ”Ґ Fire (low noise + irregular crackle bursts) В· вљЎ Fizz (wide bright noise + fast tremolo).
- **Render:** **raw WebGL2** (hand-rolled, no three.js) вЂ” 3 shader programs + **ping-pong FBO accumulation** so strokes glow and accrete; per-texture procedural appearance (fbm gradients, ripple rings, grain stipple, turbulent fire, sparkle hash). The most visually striking candidate of the fire вЂ” a glowing accreting paint canvas, the strongest pull on Karel's loved-paint lineage.
- **Why it didn't win:** continuous morph is less kid-legible than 429's discrete one-dab-one-sound; it uses 3 sub-audible LFO oscillators (marginally less "pure noise" for a zero-pitch-thesis piece); and the 3-program FBO pipeline is the highest perf/build risk on low-end phones.
- **Resurrect as:** the **cycle-2 visual deepening** вЂ” port 429's discrete foley *voices* onto 428's WebGL2 painterly accumulation canvas в†’ a noise-paint that both *crunches satisfyingly* AND *looks gorgeous*. Best kids renderer move while Canvas2D is over-represented. Refs: KГ¶hler bouba/kiki 1929 В· Farnell *Designing Sound* 2010 В· Kandinsky synesthesia. Touch IN В· raw-WebGL2 OUT В· subtractive-noise TECH В· kids non-tuned VIBE.

### `427-kids-texture-paint-grains` вЂ” granular-noise foley brush, Canvas2D *(banked sibling вЂ” the granular-texture take)*
- **Concept:** same toy; sound = **granular synthesis of NOISE** via a Web-Audio look-ahead grain scheduler. While the finger moves, a stream of tiny windowed filtered-noise grains plays; drag speed + texture control grain **density / size / brightness / spread**: Sand = dense tiny dry grains В· Silk = sparse long soft low-passed grains В· Sparkle = very short bright high grains В· Rumble = larger low-passed grains В· Fizz = rapid medium grains. 0 oscillators (genuinely pitch-less). Canvas2D strokes.
- **Why it didn't win:** solid but not the standout on any axis вЂ” granular-continuous like 428 but less visually rich; Canvas2D like 429 but less legible than discrete events.
- **Resurrect as:** the granular-texture variant, or fold its grain engine into 428's WebGL2 canvas as a "soft/continuous" mode alongside 429's discrete "dab" voices. Refs: Curtis Roads *Microsound* 2001 (granular) В· Farnell 2010 В· KГ¶hler 1929. Touch IN В· Canvas2D OUT В· granular-noise TECH В· kids non-tuned VIBE.

### `424-welcome-erosion` вЂ” Karel's REAL Welcome Home piano, long-form 5-min generative EROSION (a piece about forgetting) *(banked sibling вЂ” the intimate register + the vehicle for Karel's actual music)*
- **Question:** "What if a warm intimate piano phrase were played once, then over five minutes slowly eroded through self-feedback + granular decay until it can never return home?"
- **Tags** (clean dodge of all bans): INPUT = **audio-file** (Karel's tracks via the existing `/api/audio/{id}` door + a synth-phrase fallback; NO mic/camera) В· OUTPUT = Canvas2D (memory-strip + grain motes + fraying waveform) В· TECHNIQUE = **long-form stateful granular/spectral erosion** (monotonic, one-way) В· VIBE = intimate/decaying/unresolved.
- **The mechanic:** a pure `computeErosion(elapsed)` drives a monotonic trajectory over ~5 min вЂ” grain density 12в†’1.5/s, grain dur 80в†’850 ms, pitch spread 0.05в†’~7 st, position jitter 1%в†’90%, amplitude 100%в†’20%, reverb send 28%в†’95%, LPF 7 kHzв†’380 Hz вЂ” so phrases thin, smear, detune and fragment into a resonant wash that never cadences back. Web-Audio look-ahead grain scheduler (25 ms tick / 120 ms ahead), `DynamicsCompressor` brick-wall limiter, 5-phase HUD label (intactв†’frayingв†’dissolvingв†’erodingв†’forgotten) + a falling "memory remaining" bar. Auto-erodes the synth phrase ~2 s after Begin (hands-free). Built files: `page.tsx` (~1105), `README.md`. **Refs:** William Basinski *Disintegration Loops* В· Alvin Lucier *I Am Sitting in a Room* В· Roads *Microsound*.
- **Why it didn't win:** the strongest fit for Karel's STANDING #1 directive (use his real music) and the most poignant, but (a) it defaults to a **synth** phrase at 06:30 unless Karel pastes a recording ID, so it doesn't actually *showcase* his music hands-free; (b) Canvas2D is 2Г— in the last-10 (allowed but not the freshest lane the way 426's three.js is); (c) the erosion is granular-adjacent to 422's shatter (distinct вЂ” 5-min stateful vs 10-s freeze вЂ” but the same neighbourhood). **Revive:** the ship that finally puts a real Welcome-Home track on screen (hand it a known recording ID), or fold its erosion engine onto 422's material. Reconstructable from this spec. **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3-subsystems В· #3 named).

### `425-test-signal` вЂ” clinical Ikeda / Alva-Noto GLITCH-WALL, WebGL2 test-card *(banked sibling вЂ” the purest *refuse-to-resolve* / "go weird" swing; jury #2)*
- **Question:** "What does a piece that was NEVER consonant sound like вЂ” a self-mutating wall of sine-grids, impulse clicks and band-noise in Ikeda's cold register?"
- **Tags:** INPUT = **generative** (no device; optional density/intensity sliders) В· OUTPUT = **raw WebGL2** scanline/datamosh test-card В· TECHNIQUE = **glitch-DSP** (clocked impulse trains + inharmonic sine pings + filtered-noise bursts + a mutation engine that re-rolls the grid) В· VIBE = clinical/abrasive/monochrome/unresolved.
- **The mechanic:** a look-ahead scheduler (25 ms / 100 ms ahead) across 4 layers вЂ” HF sine pings at 8 mutually-inharmonic freqs (6317вЂ“13711 Hz), 1вЂ“7 ms impulse clicks, 5 sub pulses at irrational ratios (37.13вЂ“91.53 Hz, no implied root), and an LFO-swept band-noise вЂ” with a mutation event every 5вЂ“12 s re-randomizing densities/BPF within clinical bounds so it permanently drifts and never locks. `DynamicsCompressor` brick-wall (в€’8 dB, 20:1). Auto-starts ~2 s after load (with a "TAP TO START" overlay if the AudioContext is gesture-gated); WebGL2 fails в†’ DOM fallback meter. Built files: `page.tsx` (~908), `README.md`. **Refs:** Ryoji Ikeda *test pattern* / *datamatics* В· Carsten Nicolai / Alva Noto. **This finally realizes the В§356 banked "test-pattern" Ikeda counter-piece idea.**
- **Why it didn't win:** the purest answer to the jury's #2 (abrasive / never-consonant вЂ” the boldest "go weird"), but (a) a wall of 6вЂ“14 kHz pings + sharp clicks is a real **06:30-on-phone-speakers fatigue risk** (could read as "annoying" not "compelling" at the review moment); (b) WebGL2 was just used by 423 (1Г—), where 426's three.js is the cleaner renderer dodge; (c) builder-flagged node-churn at max density on low-end mobile. **Revive:** ship on a fire where a harsh-HF clinical piece fits the review context, or as the desktop/headphone Ikeda reference; pair the mutation engine with a non-mic input. Reconstructable from this spec. **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3-subsystems В· #3 named).

### `420-slime-static` вЂ” WebGPU compute physarum slime-mold, sonified as an abrasive non-resolving ROAR *(banked sibling вЂ” the biggest GPU swing)*
- **Question:** "What if a living slime-mold network simulated entirely on the GPU were not calm and beautiful but a roaring, ever-shifting wall of sound that refuses to resolve?"
- **Tags** (clean dodge of all bans): INPUT = generative (no mic/camera) В· OUTPUT = **WebGPU** (3 `@compute` WGSL pipelines + render pass; CPU/Canvas2D fallback) В· TECHNIQUE = physarum agent sim (senseв†’rotateв†’moveв†’depositв†’diffuse/decay) В· VIBE = abrasive/industrial/non-resolving (Ikeda/Akten energy).
- **The mechanic:** 262,144 agents in a storage buffer; per-frame agent-step (`atomicAdd` pheromone deposit) в†’ diffuse+decay ping-pong on a 1024ВІ trail в†’ a non-blocking async readback (~12 Hz, staging buffer, never stalls the GPU) extracts density / agitation (variance) / center-of-mass-pan. Those drive 5 sawtooth oscillators at **prime-ratio inharmonic frequencies** (83.2/137.7/211.3/307.1/431.9 Hz), each ring-modulated by an irrational-ratio LFO, + a Q-swept bandpass noise bed + a stochastic 3вЂ“8-bit bitcrush waveshaper + irregular burst gating в†’ DynamicsCompressor brick-wall limiter. Nothing ever tunes to a scale or settles. Built files: `page.tsx` (~1178 lines, all self-contained), `README.md`.
- **Why it didn't win:** the flashiest technical swing, but (a) **WebGPU compute is no longer a lab-first** (corrected this fire), so the headline ambition deflated; (b) its GPU path most likely shows the smaller CPU/Canvas2D fallback on Karel's 06:30 review device; (c) physarum is an **emergence-sim** вЂ” the jury flagged the emergence-sim *reflex* (#6). **Revive:** the lab's reference abrasive-GPU piece, or a desktop-WebGPU-confirmed fire; reuse its physarum compute as a sonification substrate for other inputs. Reconstructable from this spec.

### `421-solar-drone` вЂ” live NOAA solar-wind sonification, audio-only / off-screen *(banked sibling вЂ” the real-world-data + off-screen take; the natural data-lane cycle-2 to 418-seismic-pulse)*
- **Question:** "What does the live solar wind hitting Earth's magnetosphere sound like вЂ” as an eyes-closed drone that, because the data never stops or repeats, can never resolve?"
- **Tags:** INPUT = **external data API** (NOAA SWPC, public/keyless/CORS) В· OUTPUT = **audio-only / minimal-DOM** (near-black + breathing dot + big numeric readouts; the off-screen lane) В· TECHNIQUE = real-world-data audification (raw в†’ synth params, no scale) В· VIBE = cosmic/vast/unresolved.
- **The mechanic:** fetches plasma-1-day (speed/density/temp) + mag-1-day (Bz/Bt) + planetary-K-index JSON (5s AbortController, falls back to a deterministic 144-row G1вЂ“G2-storm offline sample with an amber notice). Walks the 24h series in ~75s, looping but live-different each session. **Speedв†’raw-Hz fundamental** (no scale), densityв†’partial richness + noise, temperatureв†’filter brightness, **Bz(В±)в†’detuning/beat-width that swings with magnetic polarity**, Kpв†’agitation + crackle-burst rate. Partials at 1Г—/2.0Г—/3.07Г—/4.13Г— (irrational) so no two ever land on a shared harmonic node; 1/23 Hz irrational stereo LFO; DynamicsCompressor limiter. Built files: `page.tsx` (~436), `synth.ts` (~357), `data.ts` (~111), `sample.ts` (~154), `README.md`. **Refs:** NOAA SWPC DSCOVR/ACE в†’ IMAP I-ALiRT 2026 transition (RESEARCH В§357, current this month) В· NASA space-weather sonification heritage (R. Alexander/Goddard) В· Ikeda *data-cosm*.
- **Why it didn't win:** the strongest **jury-data-lane** fit (extends the loved 418 real-data lane + off-screen + refuses to resolve), but (a) a near-black audio-only screen is the riskiest 06:30 read (the breathing dot + readouts hedge it, but `422`'s legible phraseв†’denied arc reads instantly), and (b) real-world-data is no longer a lab-first (418 claimed it). **Revive:** the obvious **cycle-2 of the real-world-data lane** (pair with 418-seismic вЂ” earth tremor + sky weather), or fold a minimal aurora-curtain visual onto it. Reconstructable from this spec.

## Banked from Cycle 356 (DEEP kids fire вЂ” ONE concept: *your body, seen through the camera, generates a BEAT, not a chord* вЂ” the answer to JURY 2026-06-08 #1 (rhythm/timbre/noise, NOT tuning) **and** #6 (camera embodiment / MediaPipe). Winner shipped = `419-kids-body-band` (MediaPipe-Pose zone-triggered drum kit). Both siblings are complete, build-reviewed, demoable builds вЂ” folders moved to /tmp and removed per the no-half-built-folders rule, banked here as ready-to-resurrect TEXT. Shared thesis (research В§356): every body-tracking piece the lab ever shipped maps poses to **harmony** (`287-mirror-choir`, `302-mirror-canon-round`, `234-kids-hand-creature`вќ¤пёЏ); none made the body generate a **beat**. Named refs across the fire: "Dance Motion-Guided Music Generation via RVQ," *Electronics* 15(10):2098, May 2026 В· BlazePose (Bazarevsky et al. 2020) В· Lee et al. "Dancing to Music" (NeurIPS 2019) В· TouchDesigner Optical-Flow-TOP lineage (for the 420 sibling). These are the natural **cycle-2 of a new bodyв†’percussion thread**.)

### `420-kids-motion-storm` вЂ” webcam frame-differencing motion-energy groove, NO machine-learning model *(banked sibling вЂ” the dependency-free / renderer-diversity take)*
- **Question:** "What if a 4-year-old's whole-body movement generated a live percussion groove with **no ML model at all** вЂ” just raw motion energy from the webcam?"
- **Tags** (clean dodge of all jury bans): INPUT = **camera (motion-energy, no skeleton)** В· OUTPUT = Canvas2D heat-trails В· TECHNIQUE = **frame-differencing / optical-flow-lite** (TouchDesigner Optical-Flow-TOP lineage; cf. lab's `221`/`388`) В· VIBE = kids energetic/percussive (no tuning).
- **The mechanic:** downscale the mirrored webcam to ~120Г—90, frame-difference against the previous grayscale frame в†’ per-cell motion magnitude over an 8Г—6 grid в†’ per-region energy + total. Region motion bursts QUANTIZE onto a ~100 BPM 16th grid (kick/snare/hat/tom/shaker), total energy drives groove fullness; a soft always-on pulse keeps a beat when still. Glowing heat-trail sparkles paint the child's movement; region pads light on fire. Built files: `page.tsx` (~485 lines), `flow.ts` (frame-diff field + demo blob), `drums.ts` (limiter'd percussion), `groove.ts` (quantizing scheduler), `README.md`. **Self-reported `tsc` exit 0 + folder ESLint clean.** Auto-demo = a synthetic motion blob sweeping the regions; finger taps inject motion as a third input path.
- **Why it didn't win:** the strongest **renderer/dependency-diversity** statement (zero external runtime deps вЂ” builds even if the MediaPipe CDN is down) and the most robust 06:30 surface, but its motion read is coarser/less *legible* than the winner's discrete "left hand = tom" drum-kit mapping, which a 4-year-old grasps instantly. **Revive:** the offline/low-end-device sibling, or as the guaranteed-build fallback if a future MediaPipe fire has CDN trouble. Reconstructable from this spec.

### `421-kids-beat-puppet` вЂ” MediaPipe-Pose continuous POLYRHYTHM (each limb drives a layer's density) *(banked sibling вЂ” the generative/textural take)*
- **Question:** "What if each of a child's limbs conducted its OWN continuous layer of a polyrhythmic groove вЂ” so the body becomes a beat-puppet you sculpt by *which parts you move*?"
- **Tags:** INPUT = **camera / MediaPipe Pose** В· OUTPUT = Canvas2D (four limb-auras + sweeping 16-step ring) В· TECHNIQUE = **per-limb motion-energy в†’ probabilistic step-sequencer density** (continuous, not discrete hits) В· VIBE = kids evolving polyrhythm (no tuning).
- **The mechanic:** four percussion layers on a shared ~96 BPM 16-step grid вЂ” рџ‘‹ left armв†’shaker, рџ’Є right armв†’conga, рџ¦µ left legв†’kick, рџ¦¶ right legв†’hat. Each limb's smoothed wrist/ankle speed sets that layer's per-step trigger *probability* + loudness, so moving a limb fast fills its layer in and holding it still thins it to silence; the probabilistic gating keeps the groove **evolving rather than looping** (the "different at minute 3 than minute 0" quality). Built files: `page.tsx` (~593 lines), `drums.ts`, `layers.ts` (`GrooveSequencer` + per-limb energy + demo energies), `README.md`. **Self-reported build clean, ESLint exit 0.** Auto-demo = sine-driven limb energies sweeping the four layers; finger-quadrant fallback.
- **Why it didn't win:** the most **generative/textural** of the three and the best "conduct a living groove" feel, but the continuous density mapping is less *immediately legible* to a 4-year-old than the winner's one-gesture-one-drum kit (a toddler may not connect "move arm faster в†’ busier shaker" as readily as "hand up в†’ DRUM!"). **Revive:** the cycle-2 deepening of the bodyв†’percussion thread once kids can feel the discrete kit (419) вЂ” graduate them from hits to layers; or an *adult* version (conduct a polyrhythm ensemble). Reconstructable from this spec.

## Banked from Cycle 354 (DEEP kids fire вЂ” ONE concept, *music that locks to your movement and gently LEADS your tempo* (bidirectional sensorimotor entrainment), attacked via 3 engines/directions; winner was `417-kids-cradle-song` (audio-only Kuramoto lullaby). Both siblings are complete, build-reviewed, demoable builds вЂ” folders moved to /tmp and removed per the no-half-built-folders rule, banked here as ready-to-resurrect TEXT. All three share the core thesis: the lab's existing movement piece `402-kids-steady-walk` only *analyzes* your beat one-way; these make the music a coupled oscillator that follows AND leads. Named refs across the fire: Kuramoto 1975 В· D-Jogger (Moens, Leman et al. ~2014) В· interactive-RAS (Hove et al. 2012) В· ADAM phase+period model (van der Steen & Keller 2013) В· Large & Jones 1999 adaptive oscillator В· Repp 2005. These are the natural **cycle-2 of the entrainment thread** (the DOM/CSS *visible* leads, vs. the winner's audio-only lead).)

### `415-kids-rock-the-moon` вЂ” DOM/CSS breathing-moon wind-down (Large & Jones adaptive oscillator) *(banked sibling вЂ” strong cycle-2 candidate)*
- **Question:** "What if rocking the tablet like a cradle let a breathing moon gently rock YOU to sleep вЂ” locking to your rhythm, then leading it down?"
- **Tags** (clean dodge of all jury bans + the SVG-4Г—/Canvas2D over-rep): INPUT = device-motion (rocking) В· OUTPUT = **DOM/CSS** (moon + stars, NO canvas/SVG/WebGL) В· TECHNIQUE = bidirectional **adaptive-oscillator** entrainment В· VIBE = JI-major wind-down lullaby.
- **The mechanic:** same bidirectional idea as the winner, but the engine is a **Large & Jones (1999) nonlinear adaptive oscillator** вЂ” phase-coupling (ОєВ·sin) + ADAM-style period correction on each detected rock peak, plus a slowly drifting *preferred period* that pulls the locked tempo down over ~90 s. The payoff is **visible**: a big breathing **moon** (DOM div, radial-gradient, box-shadow glow) sways with the rocks, slowly closes its eyes / yawns / dims, stars fade, and a green glow ring shows phase-lock quality. Built files: `page.tsx` (~28 kB), `entrain.ts` (~240 lines, full JSDoc refs), `README.md`. **Tuning caveat to fix on revival:** the constants ship INIT 1.5 s (40 cpm) в†’ FINAL 1.28 s (47 cpm), i.e. the period currently *shortens* (speeds up) вЂ” invert/retune so a cradle starting ~70вЂ“80 cpm leads *down* toward ~45, matching the wind-down narrative.
- **Why it didn't win:** the strongest *legible visual* of the wind-down (you watch the moon doze), but it keeps a screen front-and-centre, and the JURY's loudest unmet ask (#5) was the **off-screen** gap вЂ” so the audio-only `417` (near-black, ears-only) was the truer answer this fire. **Revive:** the cycle-2 "you can watch it this time" companion to 417, or a DOM/CSS toggle-skin on the same engine. Reconstructable from this spec.

### `416-kids-wake-the-band` вЂ” DOM/CSS parade wake-up with a legible "Together!" meter (ADAM phase+period correction) *(banked sibling вЂ” the legible/instructional take)*
- **Question:** "What if keeping a steady bounce woke a sleepy marching band вЂ” and the band pulled YOU into step, then sped you up into a parade?"
- **Tags:** INPUT = device-motion (bounce/pat onsets) В· OUTPUT = **DOM/CSS** parade (NO canvas/SVG/WebGL) В· TECHNIQUE = bidirectional **linear phase+period (ADAM)** correction В· VIBE = bright Lydian wake-up (legible togetherness meter).
- **The mechanic:** the *opposite direction* of the winner вЂ” leads tempo **up**. Detect bounce/pat impulse onsets from accel-magnitude peaks; an **ADAM / Mates two-term linear corrector** (О±-phase + ОІ-period, in ms space, van der Steen & Keller 2013) locks a sleepy band (~66 bpm) to the child, then a **moving target period** climbs toward a ~120-bpm parade as togetherness sustains, blended via a LEADER_WEIGHT so the band genuinely *pulls* the child up. The centrepiece is a big **legible "Together!" phase-lock meter** (redв†’yellowв†’green DOM bar, labelled "Wake the band! в†’ Keep going! в†’ Together! рџЋ‰") + a 7-member bouncing DOM parade + a look-ahead Web-Audio scheduler. Built files: `page.tsx` (~27 kB), `entrain.ts` (~230 lines), `README.md`. Lydian/whole-tone (not D-Dorian).
- **Why it didn't win:** best on the JURY's #1 *legible/instructional* lane (you SEE the coupling lock), but it's energetic + screen-forward, and #5 (off-screen) was the louder unmet need this fire. **Revive:** the wake-up / morning sibling, or fold its "Together!" meter into a *visible* mode of the winner so the lab-first entrainment is legible on demand. Reconstructable from this spec.

## Banked from Cycle 353 (DEEP adult fire вЂ” ONE concept, *a living chord that LISTENS to your piano* вЂ” cycle 3 of the a-life/JI thread, adding a "listen" subsystem so emergent just intonation assembles itself around REAL heard audio; attacked via 3 renderers; winner was `414-conchordal-listen` (inline SVG blooming garden). Three input doors: ~2s self-play JI piano phrase (default, hands-free) В· live mic ("Play piano") В· paste a Welcome-Home recording ID в†’ `/api/audio/{id}` (the `163-paths-visualizer` pattern, try/catch, demo fallback). Named refs: Conchordal arXiv:2603.25637 В· PlompвЂ“Levelt 1965 В· McLeod MPM 2005 В· consonance-sync PMC11534602 (2024) В· musicalboard.com 2026-05-05 (browser MPM/YIN). Ambition 4/5 each (#2 в‰Ґ5 subsystems + #3 named + #4 multi-cycle + #5 borderline-recent).)

### `415-conchordal-orbit` вЂ” the geometry of harmony, on a log-spiral pitch space *(banked sibling вЂ” strong cycle-4 candidate)*
- **Question:** "What if you could SEE the geometry of the pure-intonation harmony a living chord grows around your piano вЂ” pure intervals as recurring constellations?"
- **Tags** (clean dodge of all jury bans + the Canvas2D over-rep): INPUT = audio/mic-listen В· OUTPUT = **inline-SVG log-spiral** (NOT WebGL2/three.js, NOT Canvas2D) В· TECHNIQUE = input-conditioned a-life consonance-foraging + Shepard log-spiral pitch mapping В· VIBE = emergent no-fixed-scale microtonal, geometric/Ikeda-adjacent.
- **The mechanic:** the SAME listening engine, but pitch в†’ an **Archimedean/log spiral where one full turn = one octave** (pitch-class = angle, octave = radius), so octave/fifth/just-third land at fixed angular offsets and recur on every turn. When two organisms settle into a pure interval (3:2, 5:4, 9:8вЂ¦) a **color-coded chord-line/arc** is drawn between them, and the heard pitches are brighter anchor markers вЂ” emergent pure intervals appear as **recurring geometric constellations that snap into place**. Interval labels (P5/M3/m3вЂ¦) on strong arcs. Built files: `page.tsx` (~890 lines), `engine.ts` (~576), `README.md`. Extra ref: Shepard 1982 "Geometrical approximations to the structure of musical pitch."
- **Why it didn't win:** the most *surprising* viz (the structure of emergent JI made visible) and a genuinely different lens, but (a) the spiral needs a beat of decoding at a 06:30 phone glance where 414's blooming garden reads as "harmony around your playing" instantly, and (b) the spiral/constellation idea is adjacent to the already-banked `411-conchordal-spiral` lineage from В§351. **Revive:** the designated "geometry of harmony" cycle-4 piece, or fold the spiral as a toggle-lens *inside* 414 ("garden view в‡„ orbit view"). Reconstructable from this spec.

### `416-conchordal-aura` вЂ” the same living chord in PURE DOM/CSS light *(banked sibling вЂ” the lab's flagship CSS-only renderer experiment)*
- **Question:** "What if a living chord that listens to your piano were rendered as a breathing cloud of CSS light вЂ” consonant voices drifting together and glowing brighter, without a single canvas or SVG?"
- **Tags** (maximal renderer-diversity dodge): INPUT = audio/mic-listen В· OUTPUT = **pure DOM + CSS** (absolutely-positioned div glow-blobs, `filter: blur()`, `box-shadow`, `radial-gradient`, `@keyframes` breathing modulated per-node by Kuramoto phase via inline `animation-duration`/`-delay`; CSS `transition` on left/top for JS-free pitch-glide) вЂ” no canvas, no SVG, no WebGL В· TECHNIQUE = input-conditioned a-life consonance-foraging В· VIBE = emergent microtonal, ambient/organic.
- **The mechanic:** the SAME engine (18вЂ“30 organisms, kept modest because DOM nodes are heavier than canvas; nodes reused, not recreated per frame). Heard pitches = pulsing violet aura halos the blobs drift toward; consonance = blobs cluster + brighten; a CSS-width mean-consonance bar. Built files: `page.tsx` (~641 lines), `engine.ts` (~333), `audio.ts` (~409), `README.md`.

Reconstructable from this spec.

### `411-kids-copycat-mouth` вЂ” front-facing clay creature that copies your mouth, JI sing-back `[banked cycle 352 вЂ” the warmest / most kid-delightful realization; the cleanest modular code]`

### `412-kids-vowel-puppet` вЂ” Canvas2D gooey clay puppet, CEPSTRAL formants, gamelan slendro `[banked cycle 352 вЂ” the distinct-technique sibling (cepstrum, not LPC); revive when Canvas2D isn't over-represented]`

## Banked from Cycle 351 (DEEP adult fire вЂ” ONE emergent-harmony concept, *a chord that is ALIVE, foraging a psychoacoustic consonance landscape*, attacked via 3 different renderers; winner was `410-conchordal-garden` (inline SVG blooming garden). Inspired by **"Conchordal: Emergent Harmony via Direct Cognitive Coupling in a Psychoacoustic Landscape," arXiv:2603.25637 (2026-03-26)**. All three share the same engine: ~24вЂ“40 sound-organisms in continuous log-frequency space (no scale), a **PlompвЂ“Levelt roughness** fitness landscape + harmonicity bonus for small-integer ratios, **Metropolis pitch foraging** with crowding penalty, **consonance-dependent metabolism** (bloom/grow vs wilt/die + reproduce + re-seed), and **Kuramoto phase coupling** so consonant clusters pulse together; additive Web-Audio synth with glide в†’ reverb в†’ limiter. ### `409-conchordal-field` вЂ” the psychoacoustic LANDSCAPE as a Canvas2D heatmap `[banked cycle 351 вЂ” the most FAITHFUL realization of the paper's central image; revive when Canvas2D isn't over-represented]`
**One question:** what does the *fitness landscape* the organisms forage actually look like? **Renderer = Canvas2D.** The vertical axis is log pitch (110вЂ“880 Hz); the background is a **live dissonance heat field** вЂ” at every pixel row the engine probes the total PlompвЂ“Levelt roughness a voice *would* feel at that pitch given the current chord, painting dark "rough" bands and cool-violet "consonant **valleys**." Glowing agent **motes** (colored violet=consonant в†’ amber=dissonant by score, sized by health) visibly **settle into the valleys**; pulsing violet **threads** connect strongly-consonant pairs (pulse = shared Kuramoto phase); left-edge **tick marks** flag local dissonance minima (the emergent "scale" the population discovered). Side panel: elapsed / population / a **mean-consonance bar that climbs** as the ecosystem self-organizes. **Why it's strong:** the most *legible* and *faithful* of the three вЂ” it literally renders the paper's "psychoacoustic landscape," so the "chaos в†’ motes fall into glowing consonance valleys в†’ bar climbs" arc is unmistakable at a phone glance; the most robust engine. **Why it didn't win:** **Canvas2D OUTPUT was over-represented (в‰Ґ4Г— in the last 10 shipped) and thus banned by this cycle's diversity audit** вЂ” the SVG sibling 410 was the diversity-compliant ship; on pure merit 409 was the runner-up. **Perf note:** per-frame per-row roughness probing (в‰€600 rows Г— agents Г— 5 partials) is the cost to watch вЂ” sample at lower row resolution if it janks. **Resurrect as:** the next ship on a fire where Canvas2D is clean, OR fold its dissonance-heatmap *background* into the SVG garden as an optional "show the landscape" overlay (the best of both). Files were `src/app/dream/409-conchordal-field/{page.tsx, engine.ts, README.md}` вЂ” rebuild from this seed. Build-safe (client Web Audio + Canvas2D, no API route, no new deps). **Ambition 4/5** (#1 a-life consonance-foraging В· #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems В· #4 multi-cycle JI/roughness thread В· #5 Conchordal current-quarter).

### `411-conchordal-spiral` вЂ” emergent JI as GEOMETRY on a Canvas2D log-spiral `[banked cycle 351 вЂ” the most intellectually SURPRISING viz; revive as the "structure of emergent harmony" piece]`
**One question:** if living voices discover consonance with no scale given, what *geometry* does the harmony they find have? **Renderer = Canvas2D log-spiral** вЂ” angle = pitch class (one full turn = one octave), radius grows with octave, so octave-equivalents line up along a ray and **pure intervals subtend a constant angular span**. Agents are glowing points on the spiral; chord lines between consonant agents are **color-coded by interval species** (violet = perfect fifth, emerald = major third, amber = perfect fourth, rose = minor third), so as the population locks, emergent pure intervals appear as **recurring geometric constellations** вЂ” the same fifth-shape repeating at every octave is the visual "aha." Brightness = consonance Г— health; the pulse = Kuramoto phase; optional faint reference rays at just-ratio angles. **Why it's strong:** the most *surprising* visualization вЂ” it reveals the *structure* of emergent just intonation (the spiral makes octave-equivalence and interval-invariance visible), a genuine "huh, I didn't know harmony looked like that." **Why it didn't win:** the spiral geometry needs a beat of decoding (less instantly legible to a non-musician at a 06:30 glance than 410's blooming garden or 409's valleys), and it's Canvas2D (banned this cycle by the diversity audit). **Resurrect as:** the "geometry of harmony" adult piece, or a toggle-view inside the garden/field (same engine, third lens). Files were `src/app/dream/411-conchordal-spiral/{page.tsx, engine.ts, README.md}` вЂ” rebuild from this seed. Build-safe (client Web Audio + Canvas2D, no API route, no new deps). **Ambition 4/5** (#1 a-life consonance-foraging В· #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems В· #4 multi-cycle JI/roughness thread В· #5 Conchordal current-quarter).
