## В§363 вЂ” banked siblings from the WIDE adult fire (cycle 363, 2026-06-09)

Both were built to demoable in the cycle-363 fire and lost only to `437-wiki-pulse` on ambition (each 2/5 vs 437's 3/5) and freshness. Both are genuinely worth resurrecting вЂ” they answer the JURY's "refuse to resolve / go weird" mandate via inputs the lab is thin on.

- **`436-flow-static` вЂ” camera *motion energy* (not landmarks) в†’ abrasive Ikeda data-noise.** Point the camera at anything; **dense optical flow via 64Г—48 frame-differencing** (deliberately NOT a MediaPipe landmark model вЂ” the genuinely fresh camera technique vs. the lab's `258`/`419`/`423` model-based pieces) drives an Ikeda glitch-synthesis chain (continuous pink-noise data-hum + motion-gated grain noise + 0.5вЂ“40/sec white-noise click-burst scheduler + sine-ping spike detector at incommensurable freqs, all through a в€’8 dB/12:1 limiter) and a **raw WebGL2** fullscreen clinical motion-texture shader (hard cell borders, scanlines, glitch bars, centroid cross-hair). Refs: Memo Akten (optical-flow "Forms") / Ryoji Ikeda *test pattern*. **Why it lost:** camera was used back-to-back recently (419/423) and ambition was 2/5; 437's live-data was fresher. **Why resurrect:** "movement energy, not a body model" is a real, distinct camera lane the lab has never shipped; it's complete and abrasive. **Next-cycle deepening:** pool the per-click `AudioBuffer` allocations (builder-flagged stutter risk under high motion on low-end phones); consider a true GPU optical-flow pass (LucasвЂ“Kanade in a fragment shader) instead of CPU frame-diff.

- **`438-no-input` вЂ” a no-input feedback-delay-network self-oscillator (the Nakamura lineage).** No mic, no sample, no oscillator-playing-a-note: a **feedback-delay-network** (Hadamard H4 mixing matrix + resonant bandpass bank in a feedback loop) self-oscillates, kept on the edge of Larsen instability; you sculpt feedback-gain / filter-center / delay-time and the emergent tone swerves wildly вЂ” the instability *is* the instrument. Three safety layers (in-path hard clamp + code ceiling at gain ~0.93 + master `DynamicsCompressor`/`WaveShaper` soft-clip) make it impossible to blast. 10 s auto-demo blooms humв†’howlв†’hum; **Canvas2D** oscilloscope (zero-crossing-triggered) + Lissajous phase-portrait + live spectrum. Refs: Toshimaru Nakamura (no-input mixing board) / David Tudor (*Rainforest*). **Why it lost:** the riskiest of the three вЂ” the FDN runs in a deprecated **`ScriptProcessorNode`** on the main thread and the self-oscillation "feel" is unverified without a live audio context; 437 was the safer, more surprising ship. **Why resurrect:** `INPUT=generative/no-input` does not exist anywhere in the lab's 320 prototypes вЂ” a genuinely fresh category, and the purest possible "refuse to resolve." **Next-cycle deepening (REQUIRED before shipping):** port the feedback loop from `ScriptProcessorNode` to an **`AudioWorklet`** (off-main-thread, not deprecated, glitch-free), then verify in a real browser that it actually self-oscillates musically and that the edge-of-howl ceiling feels thrilling-but-safe.

## В§368 вЂ” banked siblings from the DEEP kids fire (cycle 368, 2026-06-09)

Both were built to demoable in the cycle-368 "Squish" DEEP fire and lost only to `451-kids-jelly-storm` on ambition (451 stacks 4/5: it binds today's research #5 and is the most literal answer to the jury's "loud/fast/chaotic, resolves on purpose" kids ask, with a legible energy bar). Both dodge every 2026-06-09 ban (WebGL output not Canvas2D; pitched melodic not drum-machine; loud/joyful/resolving not lullaby/clinical) and are genuinely worth resurrecting as cycle-2/3 of the Squish spine. Renumber on revival (max folder now 451).

- **`449-kids-squish-jam` вЂ” Verlet mass-spring jelly creatures (three.js).** 4вЂ“7 closed rings of ~14вЂ“18 point masses with perimeter springs + a **pressure/area constraint** so each jelly squishes flat on impact and puffs back round (Jakobsen, *Advanced Character Physics*, GDC 2001; visual lineage Ash Weeks' *Medusae*). Drag-to-fling, tap-to-poke (dents inward then springs back), two fingers play two creatures; collisions trigger **C-major** mallet notes (sizeв†’register, impactв†’velocity+brightness), energy swells the pad + lifts the register, hard-hit clusters fire a triumphant tutti chord; always-on warm pad; brick-wall limiter. Auto-demo at 3.5s. Files: `page.tsx` (~19 KB), `verlet.ts` (~8 KB), `audio.ts` (~6.5 KB), `README.md`. Builder: tsc + eslint clean. **Why it didn't win:** the cleanest, safest build, but the *least differentiated* of the three вЂ” no fresh-research bind, and the squish-toy mechanic is closest to loved `169-marble-run` (whereas 451's escalateв†’resolve arc is a genuinely new kids mechanic). **To resurrect:** the calm-but-bouncy companion to 451; or fold its per-point grab (stretch/pinch a single creature like dough) into the Squish spine as cycle-2 ("knead the jelly"). 

- **`450-kids-goo-band` вЂ” WebGL2 metaball / signed-distance-field merging goo.** A single full-screen WebGL2 fragment shader renders ~16 blobs as a 2D SDF combined with **Inigo Quilez's polynomial smooth-min** (`smin`, iquilezles.org), so the goo visibly **fuses with a fat liquid membrane and splits apart** вЂ” the fusing is the whole point; merged regions blend their hues, with glow/rim/tonemap for a lava-lamp feel. CPU physics for centers (gravity, bouncy walls, spring repulsion, fling), a merge-event detector (deep overlap + closing velocity) в†’ **F-major** triad chord-stacks; sparkly glockenspiel/celesta bells (sine+triangle + inharmonic FM "ting"); always-on F-add9 pad; brick-wall limiter. Auto-demo ~3.2s. Files: `page.tsx` (~17 KB), `gl.ts` (~6.9 KB), `audio.ts` (~7.4 KB), `README.md`. Builder: tsc + eslint clean (note: builder flagged a mid-build folder-deletion race in the shared `next build` env вЂ” verify with `next dev` on revival; the orchestrator confirmed the *winner* 451 builds clean, 450 was not in the authoritative build). **Why it didn't win:** the most visually *surprising* of the three (gooey SDF merge is a strong, kid-legible, lab-fresh visual) and the strongest runner-up вЂ” but its physics is "simple CPU wobble + merge," not true soft-body deformation, so the squish is less physical than 451's PBD; and it doesn't bind recent research. **To resurrect:** ship as the SDF-render lane of the Squish spine, or fold the `smin` mergeв†’chord mechanic into 451 (two jellies touching fuse into a louder chord) вЂ” the cleanest cycle-2 deepening, marrying 451's real soft-body physics to 450's gorgeous gooey merge.

## Cycle 370 banked siblings (the two WIDE explorers that lost to `456-kids-ferro-magnet`)

Both were built to demoable in the cycle-370 WIDE kids fire and lost to the winner on the curation gate (the winner is the freshest/weirdest image AND a grep-clean lab-first at ambition 3/5). Both are genuinely strong, dodge every 2026-06-09 jury ban (WebGL2/three.js OUTPUT not Canvas2D; non-pentatonic/resolving not lullaby; voice/pull-release INPUT not over-leaned touch), and are worth shipping or extending. **Renumber on revival** (max folder now 456). Their full READMEs + code were build-reviewed; folders removed per the no-half-built-folders rule.

- **`455-kids-sing-cymatics` вЂ” VOICE в†’ WebGL2 grain-migration cymatics (the namesake, embodied).** A child **sings or hums** and ~12,000 glowing sand-grains migrate across a vibrating square plate into the **Chladni standing-wave figure** of that exact pitch, then the plate "sings back" a warm inharmonic bell. The physics is real, not a pre-drawn pattern: each grain gets a jitter scaled by the local vibration amplitude `|f(x,y)|` (antinodes shake grains loose) and is nudged **down `в€‡|f|` toward the nearest nodal line** вЂ” the actual Faraday/Chladni sorting mechanism. Chladni field `f(x,y)=cos(nПЂx)cos(mПЂy)в€’cos(mПЂx)cos(nПЂy)`; **pitch в†’ mode (n,m)** (higher pitch = more intricate figure) across **6 plates on a D-Dorian JI hexachord** (D E F G A C, **not** C-pentatonic); loudness в†’ vibration amplitude. Mic is **analysis-only** (autocorrelation/YIN pitch + octave-collapse + 4-frame vote в†’ plate; never recorded/played-back/sent, no network). No-mic / denied в†’ a full auto-demo cycles all six figures hands-free. Files: `page.tsx`, `cymatics.ts` (field + grain sim + GL), `audio.ts`, `README.md`. Builder + orchestrator: eslint/tsc clean. Refs: **Ernst Chladni** (1787) В· **Hans Jenny** *Cymatics* (1967) В· **Michael Faraday** (1831, Faraday waves). **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: mic pitch/RMS analyser + Chladni eigenmode field + WebGL2 grain-advection sim + additive bell synth = 4; #3 named refs). **#1 NOT cleanly claimed** вЂ” `165-cymatics` (adult, audio-FFT в†’ analytical pattern render) exists; the fresh move is **voice-driven + kids + true particle-migration sim** (grains actually flow to the nodes). **Why it didn't win:** the most "Resonance-shaped" and the strongest *embodiment* (the jury's "sing not poke") вЂ” but it's the only 2/5 of the three (sits on the very floor the jury said to climb off), and its central bet (child-voice pitch-detection + 12k CPU-gradient grains at 60 fps on a phone) is the least certain. **To resurrect:** ship as-is (it's near-complete and the auto-demo de-risks the 06:30 read); de-risk by moving the grain sim to a GPU transform-feedback / WebGPU compute pass; or make it the embodied-voice lane of a "make sound visible" spine.

- **`457-kids-pendulum-wave` вЂ” pull-and-release в†’ three.js length-graded pendulum wave (grep-clean lab-first).** Pull back a rack of **15 glowing pendulums** and let go: they start in phase (a straight line), drift into a rolling **traveling wave**, and every ~40 s **snap back into alignment**, ringing a **resolving descending D-major arpeggio** (D5в†’D3) вЂ” not a random shimmer. Classic length-graded tuning `T_k = T_cycle/(K_base+k)` (T_cycle=40 s, K_base=40) so the whole pattern cycles; pure SHM `Оё_k(t)=AВ·cos(2ПЂ t/T_k)` (Galileo small-angle isochronism); each bob rings a bell at its bottom-center zero-crossing; drag-amplitude в†’ swing size в†’ loudness; always-on D2+A2 drone; brick-wall limiter. three.js emissive spheres + trails + ring-flashes, violetв†’orangeв†’cyan color-by-pitch ramp. **Self-launches on Start** (fully autonomous hypnotic cycle вЂ” the *safest hands-free 06:30 read* of the three); tap to relaunch. Files: `page.tsx`, `scene.ts` (three.js + pendulum sim), `audio.ts`, `README.md`. Builder + orchestrator: eslint/tsc clean. `pendulum.?wave` grep-clean (`196-kids-wind-chimes` is wind-driven pendulum *chimes*, not the Harvard length-graded demo). Refs: **Harvard Natural Sciences "Pendulum Waves"** В· **Galileo** isochronism (*Discorsi*, 1638) В· **Richard Berg** (Maryland apparatus). **Ambition 3/5** (#1 first length-graded pendulum-wave in the lab, grep-verified; #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: pendulum SHM integrator + zero-crossing note scheduler + three.js render + drone/limiter = 4; #3 named refs). **Why it didn't win:** equal ambition to the winner and the most reliable visual вЂ” but pendulum waves are a *known classic* (less "huh, didn't know we could do that" than a singing ferrofluid), and it's the least embodied (mostly watch). **To resurrect:** the safe, gorgeous, near-ship kids ship; or extend it as a long-form/state piece (the cycle is already a built-in 40-s structure).

## В§378 вЂ” banked non-winners (cycle 378 WIDE kids fire; winner shipped: `478-kids-wave-pond`, a genuine FDTD 2-D wave field)

## Cycle 380 banked seeds (DEEP polytonality explorations вЂ” losers, NOT committed)

### 486-kids-mood-prism вЂ” the truest Petrushka tritone (RESURRECT as cycle-2 deepening of the polytonality spine)
Twist a glowing prism with one finger; a single white drone (one key) splits into TWO fanning colored beams = two tonal centers pulling apart by the twist angle. Angle 0 = unison/white; wide = C major + **Fв™Ї major (the literal Petrushka tritone)** ringing against each other, panned by refracted angle. Canvas2D refraction fan + halo, AnalyserNode pulse, never auto-resolves (rests where the child leaves it). **Why it was strong:** the only sibling using the *real* tritone Petrushka pairing вЂ” maximal genuine tension (the jury's #1 ask), and a beautifully legible "bend consonance into ambiguity and back" gesture. **Why it lost to 484:** single-finger rotational twist is slightly harder for a 4yo than dragging two glowing things; Canvas2D-only (fewer subsystems). **Resurrect:** fold the tritone-split + refraction-fan visual INTO the two-suns spine as an "intensity" mode, OR ship as cycle-2 to give the spine its harsher-tension variant. Tags: touch / Canvas2D / polytonality / spectral-luminous. Ref: Stravinsky *Petrushka* chord, Milhaud.

### 485-kids-two-rivers вЂ” the braid metaphor (RESURRECT as the calm companion)
Two vertical rivers of falling note-droplets, LEFT = C major, RIGHT = A major (share E). A wide draggable "weaver" paddle: over one river в†’ that key clear (panned); centered в†’ both rivers braid through the mix zone, droplets interleaved, both keys ringing at full density. Pure Canvas2D additive glow + ripples, two-key drone bed, auto-flows on load. **Why it was strong:** the braiding is visible AND audible вЂ” the clearest "you can SEE the two worlds weave"; deliberate C+A (shared E) so worlds touch not clash. **Why it lost:** single-touch paddle (no two-hand play); plainest visual; fewest subsystems. **Resurrect:** as the gentle/contemplative companion to the suns, or merge the falling-droplet "rain of two keys" as an alternate visual skin for the spine. Tags: touch / Canvas2D / polytonality / playful-aqueous. Ref: Stravinsky *Petrushka* chord, Milhaud.

## Banked В§383 (WIDE non-winners вЂ” TEXT seeds, folders removed; renumber on revival, max committed folder now 490):
*The cycle-383 fire was 3 orthogonal answers to the JURY (2026-06-10) #1 ("bring genuine tension back вЂ” 15/15 consonant, 10/15 warm-resolve; build ONE piece the listener resolves through action, not a pre-baked cadence"). Winner shipped: `490-disintegration` (Basinski self-erasing loop). These two are complete, build-reviewed implementations вЂ” strong seeds for the next adult cycle.*

### 491-room-resonance вЂ” Alvin Lucier, *I Am Sitting in a Room* (1969), interactive (RESURRECT as the next adult conceptual piece)
Speak a phrase (mic, with a synthesized-seed fallback if denied/silent) в†’ the system iteratively **re-convolves** it with a synthetic room impulse response (a decaying noise burst colored by a bank of resonant biquad peaks), pass after pass, via `OfflineAudioContext` + `ConvolverNode`. Each pass the room's modal peaks compound multiplicatively while broadband speech/transient energy washes out вЂ” after ~12вЂ“24 passes the words have dissolved entirely into shimmering room resonance. You **watch it happen**: a live scrolling Canvas2D **spectrogram** (log-frequency, violetв†’cyan-white, with faint horizontal guide-lines at the room modes) shows energy abandoning the broadband texture and collecting onto the mode lines вЂ” *language becoming architecture* вЂ” plus a spectral-flatness **"intelligibility" meter** that drops as the room takes over. Auto-run walks the whole dissolution; step/replay/linger to dwell on any pass. `DynamicsCompressor` limiter; per-pass normalize; mic audio never leaves the browser (no API route). **Ambition:** #2 (4 subsystems: mic/seed capture + iterative offline-convolution engine + room-IR synthesis + live analyser) + #3 (Lucier 1969); lab-first iterative-convolution dissolution (345-speech-melody only *nods* at Lucier, never implements it). **Why it was strong:** the single most conceptually beautiful piece of the fire вЂ” you literally see+hear meaning erode into space; anti-warm-resolve (transformation, not cadence). **Why it lost to 490:** mic-dependent (fallback exists but the *concept* wants your real voice) and the most runtime-complex (chained offline convolutions, pixel-scroll spectrogram) в†’ least robust for a no-touch 06:30 phone glance; 490 is pure-client and never needs permission. **Resurrect:** ship as-is next adult cycle; consider tuning the room IR to one of Karel's published journey keys so the dissolution rings in-theme. Tags: mic / Canvas2D-spectrogram / iterative-convolution-dissolution / cold-to-shimmering-transformation. Ref: Alvin Lucier, *I Am Sitting in a Room* (1969). Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (551 lines), `audio-engine.ts` (`makeRoomIR`/`makeFallbackSeed`/`runConvolutionPass`/`recordMic`/`spectralFlatness`), `README.md`.

### 492-automata вЂ” Stephen Wolfram elementary CA as a real-time composer (RESURRECT вЂ” grep-verified lab-first)
A row of N cells evolves one generation per musical pulse under an **elementary (1-D, 2-state, 3-neighbor) Wolfram rule** (presets 110 / 30 / 90 / 54 / 184). Live cells map onto a deliberately **tense scale field** (octatonic / whole-tone / phrygian вЂ” real dissonance allowed, NOT a no-wrong-notes pentatonic); a complex rule (110 is Turing-complete) **never enters a short cycle**, so the harmony genuinely evolves вЂ” different at minute 5 than minute 1, never exactly repeating. Voice-stealing 12-voice poly synth + always-on drone + density-tracking gain/lowpass so it breathes; `DynamicsCompressor` limiter caps the densest rows. The classic Wolfram **space-time diagram** scrolls in lock-step with the audio (both emitted from the same `stepGeneration` call, audio-clock-scheduled with a capped catch-up): you SEE the Sierpinski triangles / Rule-110 gliders forming exactly as you HEAR the chord they make; columns map lowв†’high pitch, violetв†’cyan; **tap to drop a single seed cell** and watch/hear the future cascade from it. 3 s hands-free auto-start. No API route. **Ambition:** #1 (discrete elementary-CA-as-compositional-engine вЂ” grep-verified absent; `264-kids-lenia-pond` is *continuous* CA and a kids visual toy, not a harmonic engine) + #2 (CA engine + CAв†’harmony scheduler + poly synth + space-time renderer) + #3 (Wolfram, *A New Kind of Science*, 2002); also long-form evolving. **Why it was strong:** the cleanest "long-form evolving adult, different at minute 5" of the fire, structural emergent tension, robust pure-client. **Why it lost narrowly to 490:** 490 is *more radically* un-resolving (pure entropy, no scale safety net at all) and lands two starved categories at once (conceptual/critical + long-form); 492 is the strong runner-up on the same tension axis. **Resurrect:** ship next adult cycle; deepen with TWO rules in counterpoint (bitonal, Г  la `484-two-suns`), or let the live density drive a slow modulation of the scale field. Tags: touch-seed / Canvas2D-space-time / elementary-cellular-automata-harmony / cold-emergent-structural. Ref: Stephen Wolfram, elementary CA / *A New Kind of Science* (2002). Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (466 lines), `ca.ts` (`stepRow`/`makeSeedRow`/`makeRandomRow`/`population` + 5 rule presets), `audio.ts` (voice-stealing poly synth + 3 scale fields), `README.md`.

## Banked В§384 (cycle-384 kids DEEP вЂ” non-winner siblings of the explorable harmony-tension Sound-Map; winner shipped: `493-kids-feeling-forest`, camera/body navigation. Folders removed after curation; renumber on revival, max committed folder now 493.):
*All three implemented the SAME concept вЂ” a continuous 2-D harmony-tension MAP (IDW-blended chord voicings, dissonanceв†’consonance spatial gradient, no scale-snapping, no pre-baked cadence; binds **FXplorer**, arXiv 2606.08286, NIME 2026, 2026-06-09) вЂ” differing only in the navigation input. The winner uses BODY/camera (the jury's explicitly-starved depth-camera input). These two are complete, build-reviewed implementations.*

### 494-kids-weather-walk вЂ” the DRAG baseline (RESURRECT only if a touch cycle is wanted)
Drag a glowing cloud-spirit across a top-down weather world: storm corner (Bb2 + m2 + tritone + m9, heavy detune, audible beating, 7.8 Hz tremolo, 310 Hz LP) в†’ sunshine corner (C4 open fifth/sus2, 5400 Hz, no tremolo), with overcast/foggy/bittersweet (simultaneous minor+major third) middles. 5 anchors, IDW power-2 blend, Lissajous auto-demo after 3 s, Canvas2D field with lightning flicker in the storm quadrant. Clean (810 lines, 0 ts/0 eslint). **Why it lost:** its INPUT is **touch/drag** вЂ” the exact over-represented tag the cycle-384 diversity audit BANS (touch ~5Г— in last 10 shipped). It's the reliable baseline, not a rut-breaker. **Resurrect:** as the guaranteed-working fallback skin folded into 493, or on a future cycle where touch is no longer over-represented. Tags: touch / Canvas2D / harmony-map-IDW / weather-tension. Ref: FXplorer (2026).

### 495-kids-singing-valley вЂ” VOICE as the 2-D cursor (STRONG bank вЂ” high surprise, the real next lab-first)
SING to navigate: hand-written YIN-style pitch detector (`pitch.ts`, de CheveignГ© & Kawahara 2002) maps **pitch в†’ vertical** (low voice = thorny cave at the bottom, high voice = sunlit meadow at top) and **loudness/RMS в†’ horizontal** (soft = misty left, loud = open right). The child's voice walks a glowing creature through the harmony-tension valley (5 anchors: minor-2nd+tritone cave в†’ open-fifth meadow, with quartal/whole-tone/sus4 middles). Mic is analysis-only (separate context, never routed to output в†’ zero feedback); mic-denied в†’ `text-rose-300` notice + drag fallback + 17 s auto-demo. Canvas2D, 655 lines, 0 ts/0 eslint. **Why it lost narrowly:** voiceв†’XY is the most *surprising* controller of the three, but the jury #3 explicitly named **depth-camera (0Г—)** as THE starved input to pick this cycle, and camera kids pieces are loved (104вќ¤пёЏ/101вќ¤пёЏ/234вќ¤пёЏ) вЂ” so 493's body-camera navigation is the more on-target diversity + love answer. Mic was also used recently (468-bottle-flute). **Resurrect:** ship next kids voice cycle, OR push it past "one voice = one cursor" into the real next lab-first вЂ” **two children landing a consonant interval together** (genuine polyphonic pitch detection), or "lingering in the cave for >5 s slowly warms it" (tension-resolving-through-presence, not movement). ## Banked В§385 (cycle-385 adult DEEP вЂ” non-winner siblings of the **Machine Ensemble / Voyager** concept; winner shipped: `496-voyager-room`. Folders removed after curation; renumber on revival, max committed folder now 496.):
*All three implemented ONE concept вЂ” **an ENSEMBLE of autonomous machine improvisers who listen to each other AND to you, which you CONDUCT (you never play notes)** вЂ” George Lewis's _Voyager_ lineage, binding **StreamMUSE** (frame-synchronous streaming inference, arXiv 2606.11886, 2026-06-10) as the on-device lock-step generation loop, with a real PlompвЂ“Levelt/Sethares roughness meter as the live tension readout. They differ in the agent-brain + the conducting gesture. These two are complete, build-reviewed implementations вЂ” strong cycle-2/3 candidates of the new Machine Ensemble spine.*

### 497-call-ring вЂ” a RING-CANON of imitation, conducted by a SPREAD knob (STRONG bank вЂ” the spine's canon branch)
Six agents on a circle; each beat the next agent listens ONLY to its upstream neighbour's most-recent short phrase and answers with its own probabilistic **transform** вЂ” {transpose-to-consonant-degree, melodic inversion, retrograde, augment/diminish, octave displace}. One primary **SPREAD** slider re-weights the transform distribution + toggles scale-snapping: low spread = a tight near-unison round (motif circulates near-intact, reads Resolved/Settling); high spread = inversion/octave-scatter + chromatic nudges fragment the motif into clashes (Tense/Clashing) before it re-converges. Conduct by **tossing in a seed motif** (inject a 3вЂ“5 note contour at a node) + SPREAD + TEMPO + tap-an-agent to freeze (pass-through gap) or mute. Canvas2D: luminous packet arcs nodeв†’node, circle-of-fifths node hue, arcs jitter/fragment at high spread. Auto-demo sweeps spread lowв†’highв†’low. 519 lines, tsc+eslint clean. **Why it lost:** elegant, but the canon/round register overlaps the lab's existing Mirror-Canon (302/305) + tempo-canon (375) threads вЂ” slightly less of a leap than 496's "conduct collective roughness." **Resurrect:** spine cycle-2 as the *imitation* branch, or fold its transform palette into 496 so spotlighted agents can develop a tossed-in motif. Tags: seed-motif/conductor INPUT / Canvas2D / multi-agent-ring-imitation TECH / roundв‡„tension VIBE. Refs: Lewis _Voyager_; StreamMUSE (2606.11886, 2026-06-10).

### 498-swarm-score вЂ” EMERGENT chord from a 48-agent CONSENSUS + tritone DISSIDENTS, WebGL2 (STRONG bank вЂ” the spine's emergence branch + a starved-renderer)
48 lightweight agents each hold a continuous **opinion** = a real-valued pitch class on the **circle of fifths**; each frame they gossip toward the Gaussian-weighted local average (consensus) + toward the conductor's **attractor** (your drag). The **sounding chord = the emergent weighted consensus** (densest opinion-clusters become chord tones; cluster mass = loudness) вЂ” you literally hear the swarm agreeing. **Genuine tension via dissidents:** N dissident agents refuse consensus and steer to a tritone against the live majority, dragging a clash into the chord; add/remove them = the tension knob. Frame-synchronous re-voicing each beat (StreamMUSE). Raw **WebGL2** gravity-well + additive point cloud (circle-of-fifths hue so consensus reads coherent, split swarm reads clashing; dissidents hot rose/amber), **Canvas2D fallback required + present**, full GL dispose. Conduct by drag-to-nudge-attractor + В±dissidents + tempo. Auto-demo wanders the attractor + breathes 2 dissidents in/out. 563 lines, tsc clean. **Why it lost:** conceptually elegant and dodges Canvas2D over-use (WebGL2), but "chord emerges from a swarm" drifts toward the lab's existing a-life register (236-particle-life-song, 410-conchordal-garden) and reads a touch more abstract than 496's legible *named musicians you conduct*. **Resurrect:** spine cycle-2/3 as the *emergence* branch (it's the strongest WebGL2 surface of the three); or extend dissents beyond tritone-only (m2/M7 flavours), or map the attractor drag to a real harmonic-function space. Tags: drag-attractor/conductor INPUT / WebGL2(+Canvas2D fallback) OUTPUT / swarm-consensus-emergent-harmony TECH / dissident-tension VIBE. Refs: Lewis _Voyager_; StreamMUSE (2606.11886, 2026-06-10); PlompвЂ“Levelt 1965 / Sethares 1998.

## Banked В§386 (cycle-386 kids WIDE fire вЂ” non-winner siblings; winner shipped: `500-kids-aurora-tilt`. Folders removed after curation per orchestration rule; renumber on revival, max committed folder now 500.):

### 499-kids-sky-bells вЂ” the REAL sky, singing (STRONG bank вЂ” the highest-surprise concept of the fire; ship next ALL-AGES / adult real-world-data cycle)
On Start, fetches **live current weather** for the child's geolocation from **Open-Meteo** (no API key, CORS-enabled; falls back to San Francisco if location denied, and to a synthesized default-weather object if the fetch fails вЂ” always sings). Maps the live data to a warm always-on generative soundscape rendered as a glowing **WebGL2** sky field: **temperature в†’ key/register** (cold C-minor-pent/low в†’ warm AвЂ“D-major-pent/high), **wind в†’ arpeggio/shimmer density**, **cloud cover в†’ pad lowpass** (clear bright ~2600 Hz в†’ overcast muffled ~900 Hz), **precipitation в†’ soft rain-bell chime rate**, **is_day в†’ gold-day vs indigo-night palette + pad gain**. Re-polls every 60 s so it drifts with the real sky; tap the sky / weather-friend orbs (в‰Ґ64 px) to add the child's own in-key bell. DynamicsCompressor limiter + 9 kHz lowpass (kids-safe). Files (removed): `page.tsx` (353 lines), `audio.ts`, `weather.ts`, `gl.ts`, `README.md`. Ref: **Gregory Kramer (ed.), *Auditory Display: Sonification, Audification, and Auditory Interfaces* (1994)** + aeolian/wind-harp tradition. **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: live weather API + sonification engine + WebGL2 sky renderer + tap interaction; #3 named ref). Tags: **live-weather-API + tap INPUT (real-world-data вЂ” the starved menu category the jury flagged untouched all window) / WebGL2 OUTPUT / data-sonification TECH / living-real-sky VIBE** вЂ” fully orthogonal to everything recent. **Why it lost (narrowly):** the highest *surprise* of the fire ("the real sky singing" вЂ” a genuine "huh") and it lands a starved menu category, BUT its tension is **observational/passive** (the weather is what it is; tapping adds notes but doesn't *resolve* tension), which is weaker on the jury's #1 "tension resolved **through action**"; and weather-sonification is abstract for a *4-year-old* (it's really an all-ages/adult ambient piece). **Resurrect:** ship next adult/all-ages cycle as the lab's real **real-world-data sonification** entry вЂ” it's the strongest seed of the fire. Consider tuning the scale to one of Karel's published journey keys, or adding satellite/ISS-pass or tide data as alternate "what's happening right now" sources. Honest warts: Open-Meteo CORS + geolocation not browser-verified in sandbox (fallback covers both); WebGL2 not GPU-verified.

### 501-kids-hum-garden вЂ” bloom by HOLDING STEADY, not by hitting a note (STRONG bank вЂ” the freshest *resolution mechanic* of the fire)
Hum into the mic to grow a glowing **inline-SVG** flower; **any pitch is welcome (no wrong notes)** вЂ” what blooms it is **steadiness**, not target-hitting. A self-coded **YIN-style CMND pitch detector** (de CheveignГ© & Kawahara 2002; RMS gate + clarity gate в‰Ґ0.55 + parabolic interp) plus a rolling-variance **pitch-stability** metric: a wobbly/nervous hum keeps the plant a quivering thorny bud on a tense beating cluster (root + detuned maj-2 + min-7); a **steady sustained hum (~1.5вЂ“3 s)** glides the harmony open into a warm root+maj3+P5 bloom, petals open, sparkles burst. Pitch sets hue (low = warm amber, high = cool violet), snapped to C-pentatonic. Mic is **analysis-only** (connected to the AnalyserNode only, never to output в†’ zero feedback, never recorded/uploaded). Mic-denied в†’ `text-rose-300` notice + a synthesized **demo-hum state machine** (wobbleв†’steadyв†’rest) that blooms hands-free; the demo also runs on load before the child sings. DynamicsCompressor limiter + 9 kHz lowpass. SVG attributes written imperatively via refs in the rAF loop (no per-frame React re-render). Files (removed): `page.tsx` (826 lines), `README.md` (self-contained). Ref: **de CheveignГ© & Kawahara, "YIN," JASA 2002**. **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: mic/pitch+stability detection + warm bloom synth + SVG garden + demo-hum fallback; #3 named ref). Tags: **voice/mic INPUT (fresh, not in last 10) / SVG OUTPUT (0Г— in last 10 вЂ” the cleanest output-dodge of the fire) / pitch-STABILITY-as-resolution TECH (steadiness, not target-hitting вЂ” genuinely novel) / tension-resolved-by-calm-steady-presence VIBE**. **Why it lost (narrowly):** the "calm presence blooms it" mechanic is the **freshest resolution idea of the fire** and pedagogically lovely, BUT it's the largest/most-complex build (826 lines), the voice-garden register is somewhat trodden (`322-kids-voice-garden`, `158-hum-paint`), and **YIN on a real 4-year-old's high/breathy voice (200вЂ“800 Hz) is unverified** вЂ” a genuine demo-reliability risk vs. 500's permission-free auto-demo. **Resurrect:** next kids voice cycle; tune the RMS/clarity gates to child-voice ranges first, swap the SVG sparkle DOM-churn for a pooled-node approach, and consider pushing past one-voice into **two children landing a consonant interval together** (the standing voice lab-first), or **dwell-warms-the-cave** presence-resolution folded into the Sound-Map spine (493). Also a natural home for the banked **ParaBridge prosody-mood** seed (RESEARCH В§386) вЂ” let the *feeling* in the voice, not just steadiness, shape the bloom.

### 503-atmosphere-front вЂ” the planet's weather as roiling volumetric storm-fronts (STRONG bank вЂ” DEEP cycle-387 runner-up; the most *literal/cinematic* read of the atmosphere concept)

### 504-atmosphere-isobar вЂ” the weather as a precise isobar/pressure-field instrument (bank вЂ” DEEP cycle-387 also-ran; the Ikeda/data-grid read)
DEEP sibling of `502-atmosphere-veil`. Same Living-Earth-cycle-3 spine + Open-Meteo data + sustained-tension drone (open fifths at rest в†’ beating + m2/tritone/b9 as the real field destabilizes, relaxing only when gradients flatten). **Its distinctive idea:** interpolate the 12 city pressures into a smooth **pressure FIELD** (inverse-distance weighting on an equirectangular projection), take the **gradient magnitude** as local tension вЂ” **tight isobars = a storm = dissonance**, even parallel isobars = calm вЂ” and render marching-squares **contour bands + sheared streamlines** in a clean Ikeda-ish data-grid aesthetic; storm longitude pans the audio. ## Banked В§388 (cycle-388 kids DEEP fire вЂ” "Together" concept, three synchrony approaches; winner shipped: `505-kids-pulse-bridge`. Folders removed after curation per orchestration rule; renumber on revival, max committed folder now 505.):

### 506-kids-orbit-meet вЂ” two children SPIN moons into the same swing; resolution by CONTINUOUS motion-phase sync (STRONG bank вЂ” the spine's continuous-motion branch)
DEEP sibling of the shipped `505-kids-pulse-bridge`. Canvas2D; DynamicsCompressor + в‰¤9 kHz lowpass; ambient pad bed; Pointer-Events `pointerId` multitouch; 32 s auto-demo sweeps phase diff ПЂв†’0в†’ПЂ hands-free. The mandala-bloom renderer is worth keeping verbatim.

### 507-kids-hum-meet вЂ” hum to MEET a drifting partner-tone and HOLD together; resolution by vocal-pitch-lock sync, in SVG (bank вЂ” the spine's voice branch + the cleanest output-dodge)
DEEP sibling of `505-kids-pulse-bridge`. ## В§389 вЂ” banked seeds from the WIDE adult fire (cycle 389, 2026-06-11)

Cycle 389 ran WIDE with three orthogonal adult explorers, each hitting a *different* jury-named starved menu category. Shipped `508-accord-call` (WebRTC P2P, multi-user category). The other two are complete, build-reviewed implementations that were `rm -rf`'d before the authoritative build вЂ” resurrect from these specs.

### 509-spectral-loom вЂ” `queued` (MIDI + long-form-evolving-adult category)
**What if every note you play on a MIDI keyboard wove into a slowly-souring harmonic memory you must keep tending вЂ” a living tapestry that drifts toward dissonance unless you actively resolve it?** Live-performance ADULT long-form instrument. **Web MIDI** (`navigator.requestMIDIAccess`) + on-screen piano + computer-keyboard + auto-arpeggiator fallbacks (all route one note-trigger path). **Harmonic-memory engine** (`memory.ts`): each note deposits a decaying set of partials (fundamental + 7 overtones) into a ~128-thread buffer with ~20вЂ“40 s time-constants, so you hear the *accumulation* of recent playing; a slow detuning accumulator sours the field whenever it's dissonant (PlompвЂ“Levelt roughness over up to 48 partials), and consonant intervals voice-lead it back; tonal center wanders so minute 8 в‰  minute 1, never loops. **WebGPU** renderer (`gpu.ts`): a full-screen WGSL pass over a thread storage-buffer вЂ” Gaussian thread cross-sections, goldв†’red per-partial dissonance color, turbulence on sour threads, shimmer on consonant; Canvas2D fallback if `navigator.gpu` absent. Ref: **GГ©rard Grisey, *Partiels* (1975)** (consonanceв†”dissonance as a continuous spectral axis). **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ4 subsystems + #3 Grisey). **Why it didn't win:** lower ambition than 508 (no clean #1 вЂ” Web MIDI is used in the lab: 365/391/483/486), and its WebGPU output duplicates the most recent adult build (502). **Why promising:** the long-form-evolving-adult + MIDI/OSC menu categories are both jury-named-starved; the harmonic-memory "tend the tapestry" mechanic is a genuinely fresh tension model. **Resurrect** on a non-WebGPU-recent cycle, or re-skin the renderer to SVG/strings to dodge the 502 output overlap. (Built clean: page 620 / audio 156 / memory 190 / roughness 88 / gpu 237 lines, tsc+eslint 0/0.)

### 510-the-withholding вЂ” `queued` (conceptual/critical + non-screen category)
**What if a piece refused to resolve until you set the phone down and gave it your stillness вЂ” a sound you can only hear bloom by doing nothing and waiting in quiet?** Conceptual/critical ADULT piece; subject is patience and the *cost* of resolution. A sustained 4вЂ“3 suspension enriched with a tritone (45/32) + m7 colour breathes and will NOT resolve on a timer or a tap. It resolves only on **sustained stillness** detected two ways fused: **mic RMS** (`getUserMedia`, AnalyserNode-only, never recorded/sent вЂ” quiet < 0.012) AND **device stillness** (`deviceorientation`/`devicemotion` angular velocity < 0.8 deg/s). ~50 s of stillness+quiet в†’ an irreversible, once-only bloom; motion/noise makes it recede. **Non-screen-dominant output** (the starved modality, 0Г—): near-black, ONE thin breathing arc of light encoding tension via width/glow, one `font-serif` state-line ("be stillвЂ¦" в†’ "almostвЂ¦" в†’ "here."). Fallbacks: mic-denied в†’ motion+patience; motion-absent в†’ patience (no-touch timer); plus a labeled 20 s-idle auto-demo of one full withholdв†’resolveв†’reset cycle so a hands-free glance hears both states. Refs: **John Cage *4вЂІ33вЂі* (1952)** В· **Alvin Lucier *I Am Sitting in a Room* (1969)** В· **Г‰liane Radigue** (sustained-tone patience). **Ambition 2вЂ“3/5** (#1 stillness-as-input / resolution-gated-by-detected-stillness вЂ” arguable lab-first cross-modal technique; #3 named refs; could be #4 a "Stillness" spine cycle 1). **Why it didn't win:** opens a NEW spine rather than deepening one (jury provocation #2 favors deepening), and its #1-technique claim is more arguable than 508's unambiguous WebRTC lab-first. **Why promising:** the purest answer to the jury's #1 (genuine withheld suspension, resolution earned not consumed) and it hits TWO untouched-all-window menu categories at once (conceptual/critical + non-screen). **Strong future ship** вЂ” the boldest "massively bigger concept" of the fire on the conceptual axis. (Built clean: page 445 / audio / stillness / draw + README, the builder's own tsc+eslint clean.)

---

## Cycle 390 вЂ” banked siblings (DEEP "vanish into your shadow" kids fire, comb-filter / phase-cancellation)

Cycle 390 ran DEEP: one concept вЂ” *make a sound vanish into its own shadow* via **comb-filter / phase-cancellation** (the lab's first; the JURY 2026-06-11 provocation-#1 primitive that's "tension you can't hear beating") вЂ” three approaches by input. Shipped `513-kids-shadow-still` (camera-motion vs stillness). The other two are complete, build-reviewed implementations `rm -rf`'d before the authoritative build вЂ” resurrect from these specs.

### 511-kids-ghost-bell вЂ” `queued` (tilt input В· richest visuals В· needs one physics fix)
**What if a 4-year-old could tilt a tablet to slide a bell's ghost-twin toward it вЂ” and discover that doubling a sound can make it vanish?** A glowing bell rings a soft C-major chime; a translucent ghost-twin slides with **device tilt** (`DeviceOrientationEvent` + pointer-drag fallback, no permissions needed for drag). Distance bellв†”ghost = comb **delay**; a 32-bar SVG comb-spectrum strip bites into notches as it hollows; sparkle particles eject from the bell rim when full. SVG only; `DynamicsCompressor` limiter + 9 kHz lowpass; 7 s auto-demo. Refs: **Alvin Lucier** interference works; flanging/comb DSP (Julius O. Smith CCRMA). **Ambition ~3/5** (#1 comb-filter lab-first shared with 513 + #2 subsystems + #3 Lucier). **Why it didn't win:** its headline mapping (*ghost overlaps bell в†’ cancel*) is physically backwards for the fundamental вЂ” at delayв†’0 the copies are **in phase** and the fundamental is *reinforced*, not cancelled (deepest null is at delay в‰€ 1/(2В·fв‚Ђ) в‰€ 1.9 ms for 261 Hz, a *middle* tilt, not overlap); the builder honestly flagged this. Tilt INPUT is also over-used (276/500). **Why promising:** the richest, most playful visuals of the fire (two bells + sparkles + comb teeth) and the most robust permission-free input. **Resurrect with the fix:** remap so the **mid-tilt** position lands on 1/(2В·fв‚Ђ) (or sweep the bell's pitch so the current overlap really is the null), then it's the strongest tilt sibling. (Built clean: page 670 lines, builder's own tsc+eslint clean.)

### 512-kids-echo-shadow вЂ” `queued` (voice input В· most magical premise В· headphone-only)
**What if a child could hum a note and watch their own voice get swallowed by its own shadow?** The child's live **mic** voice is run through a comb filter (dry + delayed copy); as they **sustain**, the delay ramps toward the anti-phase point (П„ = 1/2fв‚Ђ) and the voice thins to a ghostly whistle while an SVG "cyan ribbon" (voice) and "purple shadow ribbon" (echo) converge and a 320-step comb-teeth path deepens its notches. SVG only; limiter + 9 kHz lowpass + в‰¤0.42 master; 7 s sawtooth auto-demo (no mic needed). Refs: **Alvin Lucier** *I Am Sitting in a Room* (the canonical "recirculate a voice until interference reshapes it" вЂ” this is the single-pass child version); **Pauline Oliveros** *Deep Listening*. **Ambition ~3/5** (#1 comb lab-first + #2 + #3). **Why it didn't win:** **headphone-only** вЂ” on a tablet's open speaker the wet output feeds back into the mic and howls, making it a poor hands-free 06:30 phone demo; and the "vanish" depends on detecting the child's actual hum pitch. **Why promising:** the most *magical* premise of the three (your own voice erasing itself) and the purest Lucier homage. **Resurrect for a headphone/installation context** (museum kiosk, or an adult "Deep Listening" version where the howl caveat is acceptable), or pair with a known internal carrier tone the child sings *over* so fв‚Ђ is fixed. (Built clean: page 770 lines, builder's own tsc+eslint clean; carries the feedback-howl caveat in its README.)

## В§391 вЂ” banked from the cycle-391 ADULT WIDE fire (2 non-winner explorers)

Cycle 391 ran WIDE: theme вЂ” *one presence, never resolves, tension NOT on Canvas2D* (JURY 2026-06-11's headline). Shipped `514-polytempo-loom` (irrational-ratio polytempo lattice, SVG, Nancarrow вЂ” tension in TIME). The other two are complete, build-reviewed implementations `rm -rf`'d before the authoritative build вЂ” resurrect from these specs.

### 516-slow-presence вЂ” `queued` (THE STRONGEST SEED В· WebGPU long-form В· the lab's best #4+#5 5/5 shot)
**What if a single living field evolved continuously for 5+ minutes with MEMORY вЂ” never looping, never returning, different at minute 5 than at second 30 вЂ” its sound and image two faces of ONE slowly-mutating presence you sit with, not a puzzle you solve?** A real **WebGPU compute** Gray-Scott reaction-diffusion field (512ВІ, ping-pong `rgba16float` storage textures, 8 WGSL steps/frame, full-screen-triangle render pass, near-blackв†’indigoв†’tealв†’gold palette). The feed `f` and kill `k` rates drift along **two independent non-repeating 7-irrational-harmonic LFOs over a 420 s base period**, so the field traverses the Gray-Scott zoo (solitonsв†’mitosisв†’labyrinthsв†’coral) at geologic pace вЂ” it has memory, it can't return to its seed. A consonant **Lydian drone** (no cadence) mirrors the SAME two LFO functions (filter cutoff + osc mix updated ~4Г—/s вЂ” NO GPU readback, cheap). `navigator.gpu` absent в†’ SVG/DOM drifting-radial fallback (**not** Canvas2D); audio always runs. `DynamicsCompressor` limiter; AudioContext in the Begin gesture. Refs: **Brian Eno** *Ambient 1: Music for Airports* (1978); **Refik Anadol** *Machine Hallucinations*; **Pearson 1993** (Gray-Scott, Science 261). **Ambition ~3/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: compute sim + render + audio-mirror + drift engine = 4 В· #3 named refs В· #4 multi-cycle long-form spine, cycle 1). **Why it didn't win:** its tension is *entropy / non-repetition*, not the jury's headline untouched **tension** primitive (TIME/TUNING), and WebGPU is the riskiest demo surface (iOS WebGPU still uneven). **Why it's the strongest seed:** it is LITERALLY the `490-disintegration` successor the JURY asked for (#2 "490 should have had children") on the jury-blessed WebGPU lane (#3, "extend the 2 WebGPU pieces") вЂ” and the lab's best path to the elusive **#4+#5 5/5**: ship it cycle 1, then cycle 2 binds a fresh <14-day reaction-diffusion / generative paper. **Resurrect as the next DEEP build.** (Built clean: 858-line page, builder's own `tsc --noEmit` + eslint clean; `/// <reference types="@webgpu/types" />`.)

### 515-two-tempos-one-body вЂ” `queued` (the audio/haptic-only screen-test lane)
**What if a piece had almost NO screen вЂ” a single presence you inhabit with eyes closed, the tension being two slowly-drifting tempi you sense in TWO senses at once: one pulse in your EARS, a different pulse in your HAND?** Cross-modal polytempo: a warm consonant drone (A2 + E3 + A3) with a soft **audio** swell at period A=1.20 s, and `navigator.vibrate(38)` **haptic** pulses at period B=A/в€љ2в‰€0.85 s вЂ” irrational ratio, the heard and the felt tempo drift forever and never realign. Near-black screen = two faint CSS `radial-gradient` breathing rings (no canvas/WebGL visualizer вЂ” deliberately anti-screen) + "Close your eyes. One pulse is in your ears, one is in your hand." Vibration API absent (iOS/desktop) в†’ amber notice + the inner emerald ring carries tempo B visually; audio always works. Self-correcting setTimeout chain for haptics (200 ms cooldown, vibrate(0) on stop). Refs: **Conlon Nancarrow** (polytempo) + **Pauline Oliveros** *Deep Listening* / **La Monte Young** (attention as the instrument). **Ambition ~2/5** (#1 cross-modal haptic-as-a-tempo-channel вЂ” distinct from `400-soundwalk-room`'s haptic-as-proximity, though haptics aren't strictly lab-first В· #3 named refs). **Why it didn't win:** haptics already exist (400) so #1 is shakier, and on Karel's likely-iOS review phone the full *felt* effect degrades to two glow rings (a visual, not the cross-modal bet). **Why promising:** the genuine audio/haptic-only lane the JURY explicitly dared (#3 "take the 0Г— lane: an audio-only / haptic-only piece") вЂ” the lab's purest test of its screen bias. **Resurrect for an Android-targeted or installation (chair-transducer / wristband-haptic) context** where the felt tempo is guaranteed. (Built clean: 339-line page, builder-reported clean.)

## В§392 вЂ” banked from the cycle-392 KIDS DEEP fire (2 non-winner explorers)

Cycle 392 ran DEEP: ONE concept вЂ” *a single warm companion you keep company by humming; never won, never lost, never resolves; over minutes it BECOMES something new, carrying everything you gave it* (the kids successor to `490-disintegration` / the `516` lane, grounded in **teamLab Sketch Aquarium / Future Park**) вЂ” attacked via THREE renderers. ### 517-kids-glow-friend вЂ” `queued` (the iOS-safe companion В· three.js)
**Same concept, rendered as a soft glowing 3D blob-creature in three.js** вЂ” a core displaced sphere with emissive `MeshStandardMaterial`, inner+outer additive-blending halo spheres, three orbiting satellite metaball-lobes, and `THREE.Points` **petal particles** that orbit the body, one per remembered hum (the creature literally accretes a halo of everything the child gave it). Color, scale, glow, orbit radii driven by the evolution state + live mic energy. Refs: teamLab *Sketch Aquarium* В· Eno *Music for Airports* В· Tamagotchi. **Ambition 3/5** (#2 4 subsystems В· #3 named refs В· #4 Companion/Presence spine cycle 1). **Why it didn't win:** equal ambition to 518 but lost on the JURY 2026-06-11 #3 steer ("extend the WebGPU pieces" вЂ” 518 is the jury-named lane); three.js at 2Г— is genuinely under-represented and clean on diversity. **Why it's the strongest of the two banks:** it is the **most legibly "a friend" for a 4-year-old** (an actual cuddly glowing being with a halo of petals, vs. an abstract RD field) AND the **safest renderer on iOS/iPad** вЂ” where 518 falls back to a flat CSS ember, 517 runs the full 3D creature. **Resurrect for an iOS-targeted kids context, or as the spine's cycle-2 if 518's WebGPU proves too iOS-fragile in review.** (Built clean: 258-line page + `creature.ts` 352 + `memory.ts` 151 + `audio.ts` 292; builder-reported clean. Two minor edges: two rAF loops could be unified; the "metaball" look is orbiting lobes, not a true isosurface вЂ” a vertex-displacement pass would deepen it. Bump the corner `text-white/40` notes link to `/55+` on resurrection per typography rule.)

### 519-kids-quiet-bloom вЂ” `queued` (the growing-seedling companion В· SVG)
**Same concept, rendered as a growing organism in inline SVG** вЂ” a slowly-branching luminous seedling/coral via a **space-colonization / differential-growth** algorithm: new nodes spawn from leaf nodes, stepping in a direction biased by incommensurate irrational-frequency LFOs (no shared rational period в†’ never cycles back), capped at в‰¤300 `<circle>`/`<line>` nodes with `feGaussianBlur` glow, attributes updated directly per-rAF (no React re-render). Growth is **monotonic вЂ” nodes are NEVER pruned**, so the organism carries every tendril it ever grew; a 32-note bell ring-buffer re-plays as a slowly-thickening lullaby ostinato. Refs: teamLab *Future Park* В· Eno *Music for Airports* В· Runions (2007) space-colonization. **Ambition 3/5** (#2 4 subsystems В· #3 named refs В· #4 spine cycle 1). **Why it didn't win:** purely a **diversity** call вЂ” SVG output is now 3Г— (`508`/`513`/`514`); shipping it would make SVG 4Г— = the new monoculture the JURY just warned about ("Canvas2D is the new three.js"). Quality was not the issue. **Why promising:** the "growing plant you tend by humming" metaphor is arguably the most *legible* "alive" of the three for a 4yo, and the never-prune growth is the cleanest embodiment of "carries everything you gave it." **Resurrect once SVG is no longer over-represented** (e.g. after a few WebGPU/three.js/audio-only cycles), or as the spine's cycle-2 "draw-then-grow" (child sketches a seed, it grows from there teamLab-style). (Built clean: 384-line page + `growth.ts` + `audio.ts`; builder-reported clean. Edge: RMS sensitivity `*12` tuned for typical mic gain; auto-demo covers quiet rooms.)

## В§393 вЂ” banked from the cycle-393 ADULT WIDE fire (2 non-winner explorers)

Cycle 393 ran WIDE: THREE orthogonal "one presence / never resolves" adult concepts, each dodging every JURY 2026-06-11 banned tag via a different inputГ—outputГ—technique. Shipped `520-singing-dune` (WebGPU MLS-MPM granular dune). The other two are complete, build-reviewed implementations `rm -rf`'d before the authoritative build вЂ” resurrect from these specs.

### 521-overpass вЂ” `queued` (real-world-data В· three.js В· the cleanest resurrect)
**What if you could hear ONE distant presence pass overhead вЂ” a real satellite, live вЂ” rising from silence as it climbs over your horizon, peaking at zenith, fading as it sets, and silent between passes?** Live ISS position from `wheretheiss.at` (lat/lon/altitude/velocity/visibility, polled ~5 s); optional `navigator.geolocation` в†’ topocentric elevation/azimuth of the satellite over the observer. ONE solo JI voice (A3 root + 3:2 fifth + octave bell partial): elevationв†’squared gain curve (silent below horizon, swelling to zenith), rangeв†’lowpass cutoff (300вЂ“4000 Hz), line-of-sight radial velocityв†’В±35-cent Doppler detune, sunlitв†’bright bell / eclipsedв†’muffled shadow hush. **three.js** dark sky-dome: 800 twinkling stars, a horizon ring with compass ticks, ONE warm-white spark with an additive glow sprite + a fading trail arc; camera drifts to follow. **Synthetic-orbit fallback** (deterministic ~4-min rise/transit/set loop) runs on load and on any fetch/CORS failure, with an honest `LIVE в†” SIMULATED` pill + telemetry HUD. No harmonic progression; the ground track precesses so no two passes are identical вЂ” never resolves. `DynamicsCompressor` limiter; no API route (public read-only fetch, no secret). Refs: **Trevor Paglen** *Orbital Reflector* (a single satellite as a contemplative sky-presence) В· the amateur satellite-listening tradition (SatNOGS / heavens-above). **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: live-data engine + orbital-geometry sonification + three.js render; #3 named refs). **Why it didn't win:** strong and genuinely fresh (real-world-data + three.js + one-presence вЂ” all clean, dodges every ban), but lower ambition than 520 (no lab-first technique вЂ” external-API sonification exists at 437/471/502) and its headline live-API/CORS is the riskiest demo surface (the synthetic fallback covers it). **Why it's the strongest of the two banks:** the cleanest *real-world-data, one-presence* seed available вЂ” a beautiful, contemplative, genuinely-new-feeling piece. **Resurrect** as the next real-world-data cycle, or fold into the Living Earth spine as its "look UP" chapter (orbital, after earthquakes/space-weather/atmosphere). Could deepen with TLE-based orbit propagation (predict the *next* real pass time + count-down) for a true "wait for the sky" piece. (Built clean: `page.tsx` 328 + `orbit.ts` 263 + `sky.ts` 272 + `audio.ts` 191 + README; builder-reported clean.)

### 522-chladni-voice вЂ” `queued` BUT note overlap (Chladni point-cloud В· three.js)
**What if your sustained voice became a single vibrating Chladni plate вЂ” tens of thousands of sand grains migrating to the nodal lines of the pitch you hold вЂ” so the tuning of your tone becomes a geometric figure that forms and dissolves but never holds still?** Hum/sing в†’ hand-written **YIN** pitch detector в†’ mode numbers (n,m) for a square-plate standing wave `S(x,y)=cos(nПЂx)cos(mПЂy)в€’cos(mПЂx)cos(nПЂy)`; 60k **three.js `Points`** grains do gradient descent on |S| toward the nodal lines, with antinode jitter; higher pitchв†’higher modeв†’finer figure; as pitch glides the figure reorganizes (mode-blended). A 5-partial plate tone + octave-below sympathetic drone sings even with no mic (auto-glide demo + slider/keyboard fallback); `DynamicsCompressor` limiter; mic is local-analysis only. Tension lives in TUNING, not roughness. Refs: **Ernst Chladni** *Klangfiguren* (1787) В· **Hans Jenny** *Cymatics* (1967) В· **Faraday** waves (1831). **Ambition ~2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: YIN pitch + Chladni field + point-cloud render; #3 named refs). **вљ пёЏ Why it didn't win вЂ” and why this seed carries a warning:** the builder claimed "first Chladni sim in this lab," but a curation grep found **`19-cymatics` AND `165-cymatics` already simulate sand settling into Chladni nodal lines** вЂ” so the headline novelty is **false**; mic-input + a 60k GPU point-count are incremental re-skins of an existing concept. This is exactly the "too similar" trap the JURY keeps flagging; the WIDE fan-out catching it is the process working. **Do NOT resurrect as a fresh Chladni piece.** Resurrect ONLY as an *explicit, acknowledged* deepening of `19`/`165` вЂ” e.g. a true 3D vibrating membrane (z-displacement + real eigenmodes), Faraday-wave fluid surface, or a polyphonic/chord-driven multi-mode superposition that 19/165 never did. (Built clean: `page.tsx` + `plate.ts` 10.8 kB + `pitch.ts` 5.4 kB + `audio.ts` + README; builder-reported clean.)

## В§394 вЂ” banked from the cycle-394 KIDS DEEP fire (2 non-winner explorers)

Cycle 394 ran DEEP: ONE concept вЂ” *your hand becomes a little singing creature (MediaPipe Hands, 21-landmark tracking); open the hand в†’ it blooms and SINGS, close в†’ it gathers and goes quiet; wrist height в†’ pentatonic pitch; nothing is ever wrong* вЂ” attacked via THREE renderers. Shipped `524-kids-hand-firebird` (raw WebGL2 GPU-particle light-creature). All three share: MediaPipe Hands via CDN dynamic ESM import (the `493`/`444` pattern вЂ” `@mediapipe/tasks-vision`, `HandLandmarker`, model `hand_landmarker.task`, GPU delegate, VIDEO mode, mirror-x); openness = avg fingertip distance from palm normalized by hand span; a scripted **virtual-hand auto-demo** that sings on load before any camera permission (and on camera-denied / MediaPipe-fail); AudioContext-in-gesture (iOS unlock); `DynamicsCompressor` brick-wall limiter (в€’6 dB / 20:1) + в‰¤8 kHz lowpass; always-on ambient pad; no API route, no guard, no npm deps. The diversity gate was decided on OUTPUT renderer (WebGL2 was the scarcest in the rolling-10 at 1Г—; Canvas2D and SVG were both already 3Г— в†’ either would hit 4Г—), so 524 won the renderer slot and these two lost on diversity, not concept quality.

### 523-kids-hand-puppet вЂ” `queued` (the most-legible-for-a-4yo В· Canvas2D shadow-puppet)
**Same concept, rendered as a warm Canvas2D shadow-theatre DOG** rigged to the hand skeleton: thumb = lower jaw (swings open with openness в†’ the dog "sings"/barks a note), fingers = ears that flare with finger spread, a wagging tail that speeds up while singing, a warm amber eye. Wrist Y (mirrored, up=higher) в†’ C-major pentatonic; finger spread в†’ lowpass cutoff (brighter timbre). Triangle fundamental + sine overtones; C3+G3 ambient pad. Refs: MediaPipe Hands (arXiv 2006.10214) В· shadow puppetry (wayang kulit / Lotte Reiniger). **Ambition 3/5** (#1 lab-first MediaPipe Hands В· #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems В· #3 named refs). **Why it didn't win:** Canvas2D was already 3Г— in the rolling-10 в†’ shipping it = 4Г— (the JURY's "Canvas2D is the new three.js" trap), and a Canvas2D dog is the least "massively bigger" of the three renderers. **Why it's the strongest bank for a literal 4yo:** it is the **most legibly-a-creature** вЂ” "my hand is a puppy that sings when I open it" reads in one second, where the firebird is more abstract; and Canvas2D is the **most permission/hardware-robust** render (no WebGL2/GPU dependency). **Resurrect** when Canvas2D is no longer over-represented, or for a low-end-device / maximum-legibility kids context. (Built clean: `page.tsx` 836 lines + README; builder-reported clean. Two edges flagged by the builder: the `computeSpread` angular formula may invert on some hand orientations вЂ” swap to `maxSpan/ПЂ` if spread feels backward; openness thresholds are tuned for an adult hand and may need lowering for small hands.)

### 525-kids-hand-choir вЂ” `queued` (the cleverest concept В· SVG five-fingertip choir)
**Same hand-tracking input, but each of the 5 fingertips becomes its own glowing singer sprite** (a friendly cut-paper orb with eyes that widen and a mouth that opens), connected by a shimmering harmony web of bezier threads. **Spread the fingers wide в†’ the five voices fan OUT into a full five-part pentatonic chord** (ratio-tuned 1, 5/4, 3/2, 5/3, 9/4 over a root); **close the hand в†’ all five slide to UNISON** (a warm hug, sprites cuddle, hearts appear). Wrist height в†’ root register (C3в†’C5, exponential); per-finger height nudges its own voice В±2% within the scale. Always-on 3-voice pad (C3/G3/E3); five voices kept low-gain to avoid clipping the limiter. **Inline SVG** render. Refs: MediaPipe Hands (arXiv 2006.10214) В· Imogen Heap *Mi.Mu* gloves (hand-as-ensemble) В· SVG cut-paper character lineage. **Ambition 3/5** (#1 lab-first MediaPipe Hands В· #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: hand-landmark + 5-voice chord engine + SVG choir + auto-demo В· #3 named refs). **Why it didn't win:** SVG was already 3Г— in the rolling-10 в†’ shipping it = 4Г— (the new monoculture the JURY warned of), AND the builder self-flagged a perf edge вЂ” it drives the SVG via a `setSvgFrame` counter state so React reconciles the **full SVG tree at ~60fps**, which may drop to ~30fps on low-end phones (still smooth via lerp, but not free). **Why it's the cleverest bank:** "hand = a five-part choir you conduct, spread for chord / close for a hug" is arguably the most *musical-pedagogically rich* of the three (open chord в†” unison is a real harmonic lesson a 4yo feels in their fingers). **Resurrect** when SVG is under-represented, **switching to ref-based direct SVG-attribute mutation** (per-`<circle>`/`<line>` refs updated in the rAF loop, no React re-render) to erase the perf edge. (Built clean: `page.tsx` + `audio.ts` + README; builder self-built `вњ“ Compiled successfully`, 4.97 kB route, zero TS/ESLint issues.)

## Banked В§395 (cycle 395 ADULT WIDE non-winners вЂ” TEXT seeds, folders removed; renumber on revival, max committed folder now 526)
Cycle 395 went WIDE with three autonomous **genre / narrative "journey-engine alternative" arcs** (Karel priority #4), each dodging BOTH rolling-10 banned VIBE poles (solitary-never-resolves 4Г— AND tension-resolved-through-action 4Г—) and avoiding WebGPU (3Г— в†’ would be 4Г—). Winner shipped: `526-jazz-room`. The two banked here are complete, build-reviewed implementations:

- **`527-cipher-score`** (type text в†’ a living performed score) вЂ” `queued`. INPUT **keyboard/text** (the starved input lane) В· OUTPUT **SVG** animated score (staff, per-character glyphs, sweeping playhead) В· TECHNIQUE a deterministic **letterв†’pitch+duration musical cipher** (D-Lydian, 26 letters across D3вЂ“A6; vowels=triangle/held at resonant scale degrees, consonants=sine/crisp; punctuationв†’dynamics: `.`=fermata, `!`=sforzando, `?`=+1 semitone rising inflection, capitals=accent) + a 25 ms lookahead performance scheduler + a continuous D-Lydian drone pad В· VIBE playful-literary, ink-on-luminous-parchment. **Named ref:** Olivier Messiaen's *langage communicable* (MГ©ditations, 1969 вЂ” an actual letterв†’pitch+duration alphabet) + the musical-cryptogram tradition (B-A-C-H, Schumann ABEGG, Shostakovich DSCH). **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems + #3 named ref; no clean #1 вЂ” textв†’music is adjacent to `119-poem-fluid`, so it doesn't claim a lab-first primitive). *Promising:* the most delightful of the three and the only one on the genuinely starved keyboard-text input; arbitrary prose sounds *intentional* because everything quantizes to Lydian. *Why it lost:* lowest ambition (2/5 vs the winner's 3/5), and "type-to-make-music" is a smaller swing than a whole generative jazz combo. **Resurrect** as a clean SVG/text piece when the text-input lane is wanted, or DEEP it with word-level phrase grammar + a second cipher mode. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (714 lines), `audio.ts` (251), `cipher.ts` (234), `README.md`.

- **`528-market-veil`** (live markets в†’ an evolving ambient drone) вЂ” `queued, with a caveat`. INPUT **live crypto-market data** (Binance public 24hr ticker BTC/ETH/SOL, Coinbase spot fallback, polled 15 s, direct client fetch вЂ” no API route/secret) + a robust synthetic random-walk fallback В· OUTPUT **WebGL2** domain-warped fBm "veil" shader (cool indigo calm в†’ amber greed в†’ violet/crimson fear) В· TECHNIQUE data-sonification (24h %changeв†’interval width/momentum, rolling volatilityв†’В±18Вў beating + tremolo + turbulence, a "fear index"в†’minor-2nd/tritone/в™­9 fear-chord fading in quadratically), one sustained JI voice per instrument В· VIBE documentary, anxious-calm, observational, never resolving on a timer. **Named ref:** Brian Eno *Music for Airports* (long-form no-cadence) + Andrea Polli / Carla Scaletti (data sonification). **Ambition 3/5** (#1 lab-first finance/market piece + #2 + #3). **CAVEAT вЂ” why it lost (honest):** its "live-data sustained-drone that tracks one aggregate scalar" concept вЂ” *and even its `-veil` name* вЂ” **overlaps `502-atmosphere-veil`** (cycle 387, live-weatherв†’sustained-tension WebGPU drone), the exact "too similar" trap the jury keeps flagging; and **Binance geo-blocks US**, so for Karel (US) it would almost certainly run **SIMULATED**, undercutting the "live markets" headline (the synthetic fallback keeps it alive but the promise degrades). **Resurrect only as an explicitly-different angle** from 502 (e.g. a *discrete* market event-sequencer / order-book rhythm piece, not another aggregate drone) and swap Binance for a US-CORS-reachable source. Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `market.ts`, `gl.ts`, `README.md`.
