## Banked В§396 (cycle 396 KIDS DEEP non-winners вЂ” TEXT seeds, folders removed; renumber on revival, max committed folder now 529)
Cycle 396 went DEEP on ONE kids concept вЂ” *a 4-year-old draws a simple doodle; it is recognized, comes alive, and sings* вЂ” attacked via THREE technical approaches. Winner shipped: `529-kids-doodle-choir` (TF.js DoodleNet в†’ 8 storybook archetypes, Canvas2D). The two banked here are complete, build-reviewed implementations `rm -rf`'d before the authoritative build. All three share: a big finger-drawing canvas; a classifierв†’archetype map; per-archetype animation + a warm C-pentatonic motif (so a "misread" is still delightful); a scripted **ghost-finger auto-demo** that draws + recognizes + sings on load with ZERO interaction and even if no model loads (it bypasses the classifier and drives the archetype pipeline directly); AudioContext-in-gesture (iOS unlock); master `DynamicsCompressor` brick-wall limiter (в€’6 dB / 20:1) + в‰¤8 kHz lowpass; no API route, no guard, no npm deps (TF.js, where used, via CDN dynamic import вЂ” the `493`/MediaPipe pattern). The diversity gate decided on TECHNIQUE/CONCEPT, not build quality.

### 530-kids-sketch-garden вЂ” `queued` (the bulletproof offline version В· WebGL2 glowing creatures)
**Same draw-it-comes-alive magic, but recognized by SHAPE alone вЂ” no neural net, no network.** A fully-local **hand-coded geometric classifier** (closedness, aspect ratio, path wiggliness, corner/direction-change count, convex-hull roundness, stroke count в†’ 6 archetypes) decides what the doodle is; the drawing then transforms into a **WebGL2 additive-blended particle creature** (600 points seeded along the drawn path: a bloom radiates, a tree floats up, a bird flutters, a wave drifts, a critter scuttles, a star pulses) that sings its motif and joins a luminous night-garden choir. Canvas2D glow fallback if WebGL2 is absent. **Named refs:** Jono Brandel & Lullatone *Patatap* (instant playful shapeв†’sound) + the **$1 Unistroke Recognizer** (Wobbrock et al.) geometric-gesture lineage. **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: geometric classifier + WebGL2 particle renderer + Web-Audio garden choir + auto-demo; #3 named refs вЂ” **no clean #1**: geometric/feature analysis is adjacent to existing pieces, and it deliberately forgoes the TF.js lab-first). *Why it didn't win:* this was the DEEP cycle whose entire ambition story is the **TF.js lab-first** вЂ” 530 is the approach that gives that up, so it clears the floor at only 2/5 while 529/531 hit 3/5. *Why it's a strong bank:* it is the **most robust** (zero network/model dependency вЂ” it can NEVER fall to a fallback because it has no model to lose) and has the **most beautiful renderer** (WebGL2 additive glow vs 529's Canvas2D). **Resurrect** as a guaranteed-offline / low-connectivity skin of 529, OR вЂ” best вЂ” fold its WebGL2 glowing-particle creatures into 529 as the winner's render upgrade (529's Canvas2D storybook + 530's glow = the ideal merge). Builder-reported: zero TS/ESLint errors across all five files. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (574), `gl.ts`, `audio.ts`, `classify.ts`, `README.md`.

### 531-kids-drawing-band вЂ” `queued, with a diversity caveat` (the most musical В· TF.js + tempo-locked groove)
**Same DoodleNet recognition, but every doodle JOINS A BAND** вЂ” each recognized drawing becomes one looping voice in a shared 96-BPM groove (critterв†’soft kick, sunв†’warm pad, birdв†’high sparkle, fishв†’bubbly bass, tree/flowerв†’pluck arp, star/cloudв†’hi-hat shimmer), all quantized to one "Tale of Two Clocks" lookahead scheduler (25 ms interval, 120 ms horizon, single shared `originTime` so there's zero per-voice drift). More doodles = a richer little song; the auto-demo "draws" 5 doodles over ~10 s into a full looping groove. C-pentatonic so every layer fits. **Named refs:** Quick, Draw! (Jongejan, Ha, et al.) + DoodleNet (yining1023) + C. Roberts "A Tale of Two Clocks." **Ambition 3/5** (#1 TF.js lab-first + #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: DoodleNet classifier + groove scheduler + per-role synth voices + Canvas2D band = 4 + #3 named refs) вЂ” **tied with the winner on ambition.** *Why it didn't win (diversity, not quality):* its "build a band / loop station" CONCEPT lands squarely in the lab's **most-saturated kids lane** вЂ” `98-kids-drum-circle`, `35/121/172-loop-station`, `147-kids-beat-pulse`, `150-kids-beat-builder`, `358-beat-mirror`, `423-kids-face-beat` and more вЂ” exactly the "too similar in design and theme" trap Karel/the jury keep flagging; 529's "your drawings come alive and sing" is the fresher framing and the more direct fit to Karel's *loved* draw/paint pieces (the recognition is the novelty, so spend it on the less-worn lane). *Why it's the strongest musical bank:* it is genuinely the most **musically satisfying** of the three вЂ” a real song builds, not just simultaneous motifs вЂ” and its tempo-locked groove engine is reusable. **Resurrect** on a cycle when the kids groove/loop lane is NOT over-represented, or fold its shared-scheduler quantization into 529 so the choir's motifs lock to a gentle pulse instead of free intervals. Builder-reported: two clean `npm run build` runs, ESLint + TS clean. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (582), `audio.ts` (322), `classify.ts` (290), `README.md`.

## В§397 вЂ” banked from the cycle-397 ADULT WIDE fire (2 non-winner explorers; winner shipped = `532-vocoder-veil`, the lab's first channel vocoder)

Cycle 397 ran WIDE with three orthogonal adult explorers on three non-saturated renderers (WebGL2 / three.js / audio-first), each clearing the ambition floor and dodging the rolling-10 banned "solitary-never-resolves" VIBE + the 4Г— renderer trap (Canvas2D/WebGPU/SVG all at 3Г—). Shipped `532-vocoder-veil` (channel vocoder, Karel's real piano as carrier вЂ” the cleanest lab-first + the standing his-real-music directive). The other two are complete, build-reviewed implementations `rm -rf`'d before the authoritative build вЂ” resurrect from these specs.

### 533-hollow вЂ” `queued` (the cleanest sculptural resurrect В· three.js В· comb-filter / phase-cancellation tension)
**What if the music lived in the SILENCE you carve вЂ” tension made not by adding dissonance but by SUBTRACTING, hollowing a sustained tone until the gaps between the teeth become the melody?** A rich detuned-saw/triangle/noise drone (E2 ~82 Hz, many partials) passed through **two stacked feedforward comb filters** (`y[n] = 0.5В·x[n] + 0.5В·(в€’g)В·x[nв€’D]`); the combs carve a harmonic ladder of **destructive-interference notches** at `f_k=(2kв€’1)/(2D)`. A 2-D field maps **x = comb delay (notch pitch, 0.3в†’22 ms log)** Г— **y = feedback depth (notch depth, 0.05в†’0.88, hard-clamped so it can never self-oscillate)**; a second comb at an irrational в‰€1.42 delay ratio (notch grids never align) produces compound cancellations that collapse whole spectral regions to near-silence. **three.js** subdivided cylindrical shell whose vertices displace **inward** at the analytic notch frequencies (confirmed against a live FFT) and swell where the spectrum survives вЂ” the carving is literally visible. A Lissajous **auto-carve** path sweeps the field on load (в‰€16 s/cycle) so it sounds + morphs hands-free; touch takes over, 4 s idle resumes. Canvas2D notch-spectrum fallback. There is **no resolve button** вЂ” the tension is permanent and structural. **Named refs:** Alvin Lucier *I Am Sitting in a Room* (1969); Maryanne Amacher (*Music for Sound-Joined Rooms*); the phaser/flanger comb lineage. **Ambition 3/5** (#1 *scoped* вЂ” comb-filter cancellation as the *compositional center* is lab-first, though the DSP primitive appears elsewhere as FX/flute-model; +#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: rich drone synth + two-comb cancellation engine + analytic-notchв†’mesh displacement + FFT + auto-carve; +#3 named refs). **Why it didn't win:** ties 532 on ambition, but its #1 is the *scoped* one where 532's vocoder is a clean verified 0Г—, and 532 fulfills the standing his-real-music directive 533 doesn't. **Why it's a strong bank:** the most *sculptural* of the three вЂ” the three.js carving glances beautifully вЂ” and a real answer to the jury's standing "put tension in a never-touched primitive" provocation. Resurrect as a psychoacoustic-tension spine (pair with 534). Builder flagged the displacement is conservatively tuned (0.42 inward max, to avoid open-cylinder normal artifacts); a subdivided torus/sphere would carve more viscerally. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (535), `audio.ts` (258), `README.md` (166).

### 534-third-ear вЂ” `queued` (the highest-surprise concept В· audio-first В· combination/difference Tartini tones)
**What if the melody you hear isn't actually being played вЂ” what if it only exists inside your own ear, conjured by two pure tones your ear can't help but combine?** Two pure `'sine'` oscillators at fв‚Ѓ (~600 Hz fixed) and fв‚‚; because human hearing is a **nonlinear transducer**, the ear manufactures **combination / difference / Tartini tones** that are not present in the air вЂ” the difference tone (fв‚‚в€’fв‚Ѓ), the often-stronger cubic difference tone (2fв‚Ѓв€’fв‚‚), the sum tone. By sliding fв‚‚ so that (fв‚‚в€’fв‚Ѓ) traces a **just-intonation pentatonic phrase** (Cв†’Eв†’Dв†’Cв†’Gв†’Aв†’Gв†’Eв†’Dв†’C, root в‰€130 Hz), a third melody emerges *from nowhere*. **Audio-first / minimal Canvas2D** (the jury's under-tested non-screen lane): near-black field, an amber orb (fв‚Ѓ), a teal orb (fв‚‚), and a faint pulsing violet **ghost** orb where the difference tone "lives" вЂ” plus a dim second ghost for the cubic. Drag the orbs to explore; 5 s idle resumes the auto-demo. An honest **"phantom only / reinforced" toggle**: by default a low (в‰€18%) reinforcement oscillator at fв‚‚в€’fв‚Ѓ guarantees the melody is audible on phone speakers; "phantom only" removes it so on good headphones at volume *your own ear* makes the tune вЂ” the gap between the two modes IS the demonstration. **Named refs:** Giuseppe Tartini *il terzo suono* (1714, used it as a violin tuning aid); Maryanne Amacher *Third Ear Music* / "additional tones"; Vincenzo Galilei; Jean-Philippe Rameau *GГ©nГ©ration harmonique* (1737). **Ambition 2/5** (#1 clean lab-first вЂ” combination/difference tones grep-verified 0Г—; +#3 named refs; #2 NOT cleanly claimed вЂ” fewest subsystems: a few oscillators + a difference-tone sequencer + a deliberately spare visual). **Why it didn't win:** the most *surprising* idea of the three, but (a) lowest ambition (2/5), (b) audio-first so the 06:30 phone GLANCE is weak, and (c) the acoustic effect is admittedly unreliable on the very phone speakers Karel reviews on (the reinforcement crutch saves audibility but undercuts the magic). **Why it's a strong bank:** the highest-*surprise* concept the lab has queued вЂ” the listener's body is part of the instrument. **Resurrect** for a headphone/all-ages listening cycle, or pair with 533 as the psychoacoustic-tension spine. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (422), `audio.ts` (214), `README.md` (109).

### 535-kids-starling-choir вЂ” `queued` (the GPU-scale technical resurrect of the "living flock that sings" spine В· raw WebGL2 В· kids 4+)
**What if a murmuration of thousands of glowing birds of light flew with REAL emergent flocking, and the flock itself sang as the child shepherds it?** Cycle 398's DEEP sibling that attacked the singing-murmuration concept via **raw WebGL2 transform feedback** (vs the shipped 537's three.js). ~2,500 agents in ping-pong VBOs (interleaved `vec2 pos, vec2 vel`); each frame an update vertex shader applies Reynolds separation/alignment/cohesion (sampling ~30 neighbours from a packed **RGBA32F** texture) and writes new state via `gl.beginTransformFeedback`; the render pass draws additive-blended point-sprite glow; a CPU shadow copy is read back async via `getBufferSubData` (`PIXEL_PACK_BUFFER`) every ~200 ms to compute audio state without stalling the GPU. Flock state в†’ harmony exactly as 537 (cohesionв†’richness, centroid-heightв†’pentatonic register, up to 4 quadrant clusters в†’ 4 sustained pentatonic voices that split/merge audibly, turbulenceв†’tremolo+noise wash). CPU-boids/Canvas2D fallback (700 agents) when WebGL2/transform-feedback is absent. Ghost-shepherd auto-demo splits the flock every ~8вЂ“14 s. **Named refs:** Reynolds SIGGRAPH 1987; Cavagna et al. *Scale-free correlations in starling flocks* PNAS 2010; W.D. Hamilton *Geometry for the Selfish Herd* 1971. **Ambition 3/5** (#2 в‰Ґ5 subsystems + #3 named refs + #4 spine cycle 1). **Why it didn't win:** the most ambitious *technically* (a true GPU flocking sim), but it self-flags genuine iOS-Safari fragility (`texStorage2D RGBA32F` neighbour texture + `PIXEL_PACK_BUFFER`/`getBufferSubData` readback) on the very iPad Karel reviews on, and WebGL2 is 2Г—в†’3Г— in the rolling-10 where three.js (537) is 0Г—. **Resurrect** when we want the flock to climb to 5вЂ“10k birds вЂ” the GPU path is the only way to scale past ~700 CPU agents. Built files (removed): `boids.ts` (918), `page.tsx` (306), `audio.ts` (244), `README.md`.

### 536-kids-lantern-shoal вЂ” `queued` (the best-legibility resurrect / character-art donor for 537 В· Canvas2D В· kids 4+)
**What if a shoal of big, friendly glowing lantern-fish swam together with real flocking, each fish a little FRIEND with eyes and a tail of light вЂ” and the shoal sang as a 4-year-old herds it?** Cycle 398's DEEP sibling вЂ” the same singing-murmuration concept on **Canvas2D** with **rich per-creature character** (radial-gradient glow bodies, simple eyes, dot/bezier tails, additive `'lighter'` glow), ~380 fish so each reads as an individual. Spatial-hash boids (Reynolds; 80 px cells; velocity clamp 40вЂ“180 px/s; boundary repulsion); touch lure (single + two-finger split) + optional device-tilt "current." Shoal state в†’ harmony as 537 (cohesionв†’warmth, centroid-Yв†’register, up to 3 k-means clusters в†’ sustained pentatonic voices, speedв†’tremolo). Ghost-lure auto-demo splits the shoal every ~8 s. **Named refs:** Reynolds SIGGRAPH 1987; Reynolds GDC 1999 *Steering Behaviors*; Partridge 1982 *The structure and function of fish schools*. **Ambition 3/5** (#2+#3+#4). **Why it didn't win вЂ” diversity, not quality:** the **best literal-4yo legibility** of the three (you can see individual friends moving together), but Canvas2D was already 3Г— in the rolling-10 and shipping it would push Canvas2D to **4Г—** вЂ” the monoculture trap. **Resurrect** when Canvas2D is scarce again, OR fold its character-art (eyes/tails) into 537's `THREE.Points` so the murmuration's birds read as individuals. Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (575), `shoal.ts` (311), `audio.ts` (226), `README.md`.

### 539-tremor-globe вЂ” `queued` (banked WIDE non-winner, cycle 399 В· live USGS earthquake sonification В· three.js globe В· adult)
**What if Resonance made music about the living Earth вЂ” sonifying real, live earthquakes so you inhabit one planetary presence that never stops trembling?** Fetches the public CORS-open **USGS real-time GeoJSON feed** (`.../summary/all_day.geojson`, no key, re-polled ~90s) + a 20-quake embedded fallback. Each quake в†’ an audio event: **magnitudeв†’pitch+loudness+duration** (M0в‰€420 Hz bell в†’ M8в‰€28 Hz groan), **depthв†’lowpass timbre**, **longitudeв†’stereo pan**; a stochastic wave-scheduler fires 3вЂ“8 events every ~18 s over an 8 s window with downward pitch-glide, over a 16 Hz sub-bass drone that breathes with the dataset's mean magnitude. three.js Fibonacci dot-sphere globe auto-rotates; markers flare in sync. Voice pool capped at 8. **Named refs:** USGS feeds; Andrea Polli *Atmospherics/Weather Works*; Florian Dombois *Auditory Seismology*; Carla Scaletti. **Why it didn't win (cycle 399):** its ambition-#1 claim ("first real external-API sonification") is **false** вЂ” the lab already has `233-earth-pulse`, `314-solar-wind`, `437-wiki-pulse`, `463-terra-gamelan`, and `337-seismic-globe` (a near-direct sibling) вЂ” so it falls to #2+#3=2/5 and is the most *redundant* of the three explorers. Competently built (1,135 lines, 4 subsystems, build-clean in isolation). **Resurrect** only if it differentiates hard from 337/233 вЂ” e.g. drop the globe entirely for a non-screen audio-only Earth-drone, or sonify a feed the lab hasn't (live lightning/Blitzortung, ISS pass, ocean-buoy wave-height). Built files (removed): `page.tsx` (323), `audio.ts` (263), `globe.ts` (298), `quakes.ts` (112), `README.md`.

### 540-slime-cantor вЂ” `queued` (banked WIDE non-winner, cycle 399 В· WebGPU Physarum transport network В· adult)
**What if Resonance grew a single living organism вЂ” a Physarum slime-mold transport network on the GPU вЂ” and the shape of the network it builds IS the evolving voice?** Jeff Jones (2010) agent sense-steer-deposit + diffuse-decay on WebGPU compute (WebGL2 / CPU-Canvas2D fallback); field statistics (coverageв†’brightness, connectednessв†’consonance, turbulenceв†’tremolo) drive a long-form never-resolving drone; pointer = food-source attractor. **Named refs:** Jeff Jones *Artificial Life* 2010; Sage Jenson (mxsage) "38"/Physarum; Toshiyuki Nakagaki (Nature 2000); Refik Anadol. **Why it didn't win (cycle 399):** (1) its ambition-#1 ("first physarum / raw-GPU compute") is **false** вЂ” `327-physarum-choir` already exists (plus WebGPU at 486/518/520), so physarum is not lab-first; (2) at curation time it *looked* incomplete (only `audio.ts` + `sim.ts` written) вЂ” **corrected post-commit:** a second, very slow 540 builder (~34 min) actually finished it fully (`page.tsx` 213 / `sim.ts` 935 / `audio.ts` 199 / `README.md` 172) with all three GPU paths (WGSL 65k agents / WebGL2 16k / CPU 3k), so it was *late*, not broken вЂ” but the false #1 stands regardless; (3) its late-finishing agent kept re-materializing its folder *after* every removal (incl. after the commit) and broke the first authoritative build (its triple-slash `webgpu.d.ts` path-reference fails ESLint) вЂ” a worse repeat of the cycle-398 race. **Resurrect** only with a *differentiated* angle vs 327 (e.g. two organisms competing for one food field = back toward "two parties", or physarum solving a maze shaped by the live audio spectrum) AND `TaskStop` the agent before removing its folder. Built files (removed): full `page.tsx`/`sim.ts`/`audio.ts`/`README.md`.

### 542-kids-liquid-light-gl вЂ” `queued` (banked DEEP non-winner, cycle 400 В· WebGL2 ping-pong stable-fluids В· kids 4+)
**Same "singing liquid light" concept as the shipped `541-kids-liquid-light`, but on WebGL2 instead of WebGPU.** A full Jos Stam (SIGGRAPH 1999) stable-fluids solver implemented in **WebGL2 fragment shaders with ping-pong half-float FBOs**: splat в†’ curl в†’ **vorticity confinement** в†’ divergence в†’ 24-iter Jacobi pressure в†’ gradient-subtract в†’ velocity & dye advection в†’ luminous tone-mapped display with cheap bloom. Same kids-safe pentatonic sonification (swirlв†’brightness, heightв†’register, C3вЂ“C5, always-on pad, в€’6 dB/20:1 limiter), throttled (~15 Hz) `gl.readPixels` energy sampling (NOT per-frame), ghost-finger auto-demo, Canvas2D "lite fluid" fallback, `text-rose-300` notice. **Why it didn't win (cycle 400):** lost purely on the **diversity audit** вЂ” WebGL2 is at 2Г— in the kids rolling-10 (524/500) and Canvas2D-class renderers are crowding toward 4Г—, while WebGPU was 0Г—; the winner's WebGPU path is the harder diversification. It is complete + clean (`page.tsx` 332, `fluid-gl.ts` w/ vorticity, `fallback.ts`, `audio.ts`, README). **Resurrect** as the **iPad-reliable production path** if Karel reports the WebGPU `541` doesn't run on his device вЂ” WebGL2 is far more uniformly supported on iOS Safari than WebGPU. `CURL_AMT`/dissipation/splat-radius are eyeballed and want a real-GPU tuning pass. Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `fluid-gl.ts`, `fallback.ts`, `audio.ts`, `README.md`.

### 543-kids-liquid-light-flow вЂ” `queued` (banked DEEP non-winner, cycle 400 В· Canvas2D particle-advection В· kids 4+)
**The most-compatible "singing liquid light" approach: no GPU shaders at all.** A coarse **56Г—56 velocity grid** the finger stirs (impulse splats + diffuse + decay) carrying a slow ambient **curl-noise** (Bridson et al. 2007) so the pool always swirls on its own, advecting **~6500 glowing dye particles** rendered additively (`globalCompositeOperation = "lighter"`) over a low-alpha dark fade-trail в†’ ink-in-water tails, not dots. Same kids-safe pentatonic sonification + always-on pad + ghost-finger auto-demo; tuned for в‰Ґ30 fps on older iPads (particle count is the obvious knob). **Why it didn't win (cycle 400):** lost as **essentially the winner's own Canvas2D fallback** promoted to a standalone piece вЂ” and Canvas2D is trending toward 4Г— in the kids window. It is the best legibility/compatibility option and genuinely reads as flowing liquid. **Resurrect** if a future cycle wants a *zero-GPU* guaranteed-everywhere kids fluid, or fold its 56Г—56-grid + 6500-particle tuning into `541`'s fallback to upgrade the lite path. Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `flow.ts`, `audio.ts`, `README.md`.

### 544-conductors-canon вЂ” `queued` (banked DEEP non-winner, cycle 401 В· MediaPipe Hands two-hand conducting в†’ SVG scrolling loom В· adults / polytempo)
**The literal "conduct the loom with your two hands."** Cycle 2 of `514-polytempo-loom` via MediaPipe Hands: each hand is one conductor вЂ” its vertical wrist/fingertip trajectory is read for "visual beats" (downward velocity-reversal at the ictus, В±0.04 normalized-Y threshold), inter-beat intervals (0.35вЂ“1.55 s = 40вЂ“170 BPM) averaged over 3вЂ“5 beats and smoothed (П„=1.5 s, never quantized). Left hand в†’ voices 0вЂ“1 (Г—1, Г—1/в€љ2), right hand в†’ voices 2вЂ“4 (Г—1, Г—1/П†, Г—П†/2) в†’ a conducted 5-voice Nancarrow canon on the same "Tale of Two Clocks" lookahead engine + D-pentatonic bell timbre + в€’12 dBFS brick-wall limiter as the winner. Renders in **514's exact SVG scrolling loom** (5 color-coded lanes, marks scroll at 58 px/s, NOW line at 22%, glow on fire, direct-DOM mutation вЂ” zero React re-renders) so it reads instantly as "514, but now I conduct it." Ghost conductors (72 & 72в€љ2 BPM) drive it from frame one; resume after 4 s of no hands. MediaPipe via `webpackIgnore` CDN dynamic import (`@mediapipe/tasks-vision@0.10.14`, no npm dep); careful self-report (helpers non-`use*`, the two MediaPipe `any` casts `eslint-disable`'d, exhaustive-deps obeyed). Files (removed): `page.tsx` (1081), `README.md` (169). **Ambition 3/5** (#2 + #3 Nancarrow/SMT + #4 514 cycle 2; #1 contestable вЂ” MediaPipe Hands used at 524, beat detection at 106/147). **Why it didn't win (cycle 401):** diversity audit вЂ” SVG is already 3Г— in the jury rolling-15 (508/514/538), so shipping it would push SVG to **4Г— = newly over-represented**, the exact renderer-monoculture the jury is fighting; the winner's three.js (1Г—) lowers concentration instead. **Resurrect FIRST** if Karel wants the literal two-hand conducting, or if the winner's three.js / no-ML motionв†’tempo underperforms on his device вЂ” this is near-shippable and its hand-beat detection is likely more responsive than autocorrelation-on-optical-flow. Unverified: the В±0.04 beat threshold wants real-gesture tuning; left/right hand assignment uses an x-position heuristic (mirrored feeds can invert).

### 546-clock-canon вЂ” `queued` (banked DEEP non-winner, cycle 401 В· MediaPipe Pose full-body two-arm conducting в†’ SVG orbital phase-clock В· adults / polytempo)
**Your whole body conducts the canon, and you watch it as orbiting clock-hands that sweep and NEVER realign.** Cycle 2 of `514-polytempo-loom` via MediaPipe Pose (full-body, works at a distance, dance-like): left wrist (landmark 15) vs right wrist (16) vertical beat в†’ two conducted tempi (same visual-beat ictus detection + smoothing as 544), driving the same 5-voice "Tale of Two Clocks" Nancarrow engine. The distinguishing move is a **fresh visual idiom** (not 514's scrolling loom): each voice is a **dot orbiting a circle** at angular velocity = its tempo (one revolution per beat); incommensurable rates mean the dots sweep and never realign вЂ” the *visual proof of the math* вЂ” with fading trails, a glow/pulse as each dot crosses 12 o'clock, and a **phase-proximity chord** that brightens between two dots when they near-align (a near-miss, NOT a downbeat вЂ” implements 514's own "phase proximity heatmap" cycle-2 hook). Ghost arms (72 & 72в€љ2 BPM) sweep from frame one; resume after 4 s of no body. MediaPipe Pose via `webpackIgnore` CDN import (`pose_landmarker_lite`, no npm dep). Complete (`page.tsx` ~39.5 KB, `README.md` ~6.8 KB; its builder's "completed" notification arrived before the files flushed вЂ” a delayed-write race, handled). **Ambition 3/5** (#2 + #3 Nancarrow/SMT + #4 514 cycle 2; #1 contestable вЂ” Pose used at 493). **Why it didn't win (cycle 401):** same SVG-would-hit-4Г— diversity reason as 544, AND full-body Pose is the least reliable of the three at the 06:30 phone-glance distance (the winner's no-ML room-motion needs no body in frame). **Resurrect** for the **orbital-clock visual itself** вЂ” the clock-hands-that-never-realign is arguably the most legible single image of "incommensurable tempi" in the whole spine; fold it into 545/544 as an alternate view, or ship it when SVG is scarce again. Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `README.md`.

### 571-the-withholding вЂ” `queued` (banked WIDE non-winner, cycle 411 В· mic-silence inverse-gate В· minimal SVG В· adult / conceptual-critical)
**What if there were a piece of music you could only hear by GIVING SOMETHING UP вЂ” a composition that exists only inside your restraint, playing only while the room stays silent and withdrawing the instant you make a sound?** The ordinary listener relationship (press play, receive) is inverted: the visitor must continuously *earn* the sound by withholding speech/movement/coughs. Mic `AnalyserNode` RMS read as an **inverse gate**: below a quiet threshold a 0..1 "depth" state integrates UP and the drone reveals more voices one by one (root в†’ fifth в†’ octave в†’ third в†’ upper partials, just-intonation above A2/110 Hz, multi-second `setTargetAtTime` swells); any sound above threshold makes depth DECAY and the upper voices fade вЂ” so the piece is audibly different after ~60s of sustained silence than at second 5. Minimal SVG: a single slowly-breathing aura that brightens as the music is "received" and contracts on interruption, a depth bar, voice indicators, and a kind `text-white/75` "you made a sound вЂ” it withdrew" notice for unmistakable cause/effect. Master `gain в†’ lowpass в†’ DynamicsCompressor в†’ destination`, quiet + warm. Mic-denied OR noisy-room в†’ an **"imagine the silence"** button raises depth on a slow timer so the full reveal still plays in a ~20s glance. **Named refs:** John Cage *4'33"* (1952); Christine Sun Kim (sound/silence and the cost of access); Manfred Werder / Wandelweiser (extreme quiet as material); Jem Finer *Longplayer* (patience as medium). **Ambition 2вЂ“3/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: inverse mic-gate + stateful integrating reveal + JI drone synth + SVG render; #3 named refs above; **#1 contestable** вЂ” a *conceptual/critical* category the lab has barely touched, but localStorage/state isn't a novel *technique*). **Why it didn't win (cycle 411):** the **strongest pure concept** of the three and the cleanest fill for the genuinely-missing conceptual/critical lane the jury's menu keeps daring (#3 non-screen-ish, #2 silence-not-physical-field) вЂ” but its payoff requires either a quiet room or pressing the demo button, making it the **least glance-legible** at a 06:30 silent phone review, where 570's auto-demo simply speaks-and-sings itself. **Resurrect FIRST** when a WIDE cycle wants the conceptual lane and language/voice is crowded вЂ” it is near-shippable. Self-flagged rough edges: `setTargetAtTime` called every RAF frame (throttle to ~100ms); breathing animation drives off `performance.now()` so it drifts vs the audio envelope (aesthetically OK, not intentional). Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `README.md`.

### 572-orrery-tunings вЂ” `queued` (banked WIDE non-winner, cycle 411 В· device-orientation gyro В· raw WebGL2 aurora shader В· adult / meditative-spatial)
**What if you held your phone up and slowly turned and tilted through the room to tune into invisible "stations" of a just-intonation harmonic sky вЂ” so navigating PHYSICAL space (where you point) navigates HARMONIC space (which pure-ratio chord you hear)?** `DeviceOrientationEvent` (alpha/beta/gamma; iOS 13+ `requestPermission()` inside the Start tap) places 7 just-intonation stations (1/1, 9/8, 5/4, 4/3, 3/2, 5/3, 15/8) at specific compass headings + tilts across the celestial sphere; the current heading/tilt picks a **great-circle inverse-distance-weighted blend** of the nearest stations в†’ a smoothly crossfaded just chord (root osc + partial bank at EXACT rational ratios, `setTargetAtTime` ~0.3вЂ“0.6s crossfades). Holding still near a station в†’ a clean beating-free pure chord + a "Lock %" climbs to 100; between stations в†’ a richer tense blend. **Raw hand-written WebGL2 GLSL ES 3.00** fullscreen-triangle aurora whose brightest warped region tracks the tuned-in direction; compass-rose SVG HUD + station/ratio readout. Fallbacks: desktop pointer-drag "look around"; no-input auto-demo pans through all 7 stations; WebGL2-absent в†’ `text-rose-300` + CSS-gradient that still shifts hue with heading. **Named refs:** La Monte Young & Marian Zazeela *Dream House* (a sustained-JI environment you move through); Pauline Oliveros *Deep Listening*; Maryanne Amacher (sound that changes as you move your head); Harry Partch / Ben Johnston (JI ratio lattices). **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: orientation input + JI oscillator bank + IDW field math + WebGL2 shader; #3 named refs above; **no clean #1** вЂ” gyro [238/253/308/вЂ¦], JI synthesis, and "a sound-room you move through" [394-soundfield-room/400-soundwalk-room/441/475/486/496/552] are all well-trodden in the lab). **Why it didn't win (cycle 411):** the **lowest ambition + most conceptually redundant** of the three (it's a navigable variant of the many soundfield/tilt/JI-room pieces), and the builder self-flags a **6-octave FBM domain-warp evaluated 2Г— for warp + 2Г— for the curtain** that "may drop frames on older iPads" вЂ” the exact device Karel reviews on. **Resurrect** only with a hard differentiator: derive the station headings from a *principled projection of the 5-limit lattice onto the sphere* (not artistic placement), and a much lighter shader (single-octave warp / precomputed gradient). Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `field.ts`, `README.md`.

### 578-magnetosphere вЂ” `queued` (banked WIDE non-winner, cycle 413 В· live NOAA space-weather data В· WebGPU compute aurora В· adult / awe-contemplative) вЂ” **RESURRECT FIRST (next non-adjacent-to-data adult cycle)**

Live HUD shows the real Kp / wind / Bz + timestamp + a LIVE-vs-sample badge; auto-fetches + auto-plays a gentle demo on load (one tap to unlock audio) вЂ” the **best phone-glance** of the three. **Named refs:** Andrea Polli (*Sonic Antarctica* / space-weather sonification); Semiconductor (*Brilliant Noise* вЂ” raw solar data); Brian Eno (generative recombination); NASA/CARISMA sonification lineage. **Ambition 3вЂ“4/5** (#1 first live geomagnetic/space-weather sonification AND a WebGPU-compute generative-data piece; #2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: multi-endpoint live fetch + look-ahead scheduler synth + WebGPU compute aurora; #3 named refs; #5 ties WebGPU's now-cross-browser-shipped status, Safari 26 / Firefox 141). **Why it didn't win (cycle 413):** the **highest raw ambition + best glance**, and it would **revive WebGPU** (jury-starved at 1Г—, explicitly wanted back) вЂ” but its input modality (real-world-data API в†’ generative music) **repeats the immediately prior cycle's `575-kids-sky-song`** (weatherв†’generative), the cross-cycle "too similar" trap. **Resurrect FIRST** on the next adult cycle that is NOT adjacent to a data-sonification ship вЂ” it directly serves jury #5 (WebGPU) + the standing data-sonification menu, in a different register (invisible magnetosphere, adult, WebGPU) from 575. ### 577-still-bloom вЂ” `queued` (banked WIDE non-winner, cycle 413 В· device-motion stillness В· audio-first + minimal Canvas2D В· adult / warm-meditative)
**What if music only blooms when you go STILL вЂ” hold yourself (and your phone) calm and a warm drone slowly unfolds voice by voice; move and it gently recedes вЂ” so the piece rewards stillness, not action?** A "stillness depth" in [0,1] integrates UP when `DeviceMotionEvent.accelerationIncludingGravity` jitter (high-passed magnitude variance) is low and DECAYS on movement (desktop fallback: pointer-speed proxy). Depth crossings reveal an additive **just-intonation drone** voice-by-voice over a warm A2/110 Hz root (1/1 в†’ 2/1 в†’ 3/2 в†’ 5/4 в†’ 9/8 в†’ 5/2 в†’ 15/8), each with multi-second `setTargetAtTime` swells (throttled ~90ms вЂ” fixes 571's per-frame bug) + per-voice/filter drift LFOs so it never loops and is audibly fuller after 60s than at second 5. **Audio-first** (the 0Г— off-glass lane): only a minimal **Canvas2D** breathing warm aura + voice ring + depth bar. Master `gain в†’ lowpass в†’ DynamicsCompressor в†’ destination`, quiet + warm. iOS `DeviceMotionEvent.requestPermission()` fired synchronously in the Start tap; denied/unavailable в†’ pointer-stillness; neither в†’ an "imagine you're still" auto-demo blooms within ~25s and cancels on real input. **Named refs:** Г‰liane Radigue (*Trilogie de la Mort* вЂ” extremely slow drone drift); Pauline Oliveros *Deep Listening*; La Monte Young (sustained tones). **Ambition 2/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems: motion-stillness sensing + stateful integrating gate + long-form JI additive synth + Canvas2D aura; #3 named refs; no clean #1 вЂ” stillness-as-input is conceptual, not a novel *technique*). **Why it didn't win (cycle 413):** the **warmest + cleanest fill for the off-glass / audio-only lane** the jury keeps daring (#1 "spend a cycle off the glass entirely"), but the **lowest ambition** of the three and conceptually adjacent to banked **`571-the-withholding`** (mic-silence inverse-gate в†” motion-stillness gate вЂ” same "earn the sound by restraint" spine, different sensor). **Resurrect** when an adult cycle wants the genuine audio-only lane and the silence/restraint concept hasn't shipped recently вЂ” give it a hard differentiator vs 571 (e.g. the stillness *teaches* a slow breath rhythm, or ties to real circadian/HRV-style data). Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `motion.ts`, `README.md`.

---

## В§414 banked seeds (cycle 414, KIDS DEEP вЂ” one concept, *a luminous elastic sheet you grab and stretch; its tension bends a CONTINUOUS warm chord*, via three renderer/interaction approaches; both losers build-complete [clean tsc+eslint in isolation], `rm -rf`'d after losing to `579-silk-choir`; resurrect by re-spawning the brief, renumber on revival вЂ” max committed folder now 579)

Cycle 414 fired a **kids DEEP** triple off ONE fresh concept вЂ” *grab a luminous sheet of light and pull it like silk; the membrane's tension (verlet / position-based dynamics) bends a warm choir/bowed-string chord вЂ” you bend the chord with your hands, you never tap a discrete note.* The directest break from JURY 2026-06-13's banned kids **pentatonic-tap-wash** (в‰€6 of 7 kids pieces are "tap в†’ a discrete consonant note в†’ pretty viz"), on the **jury-starved WebGPU** renderer it explicitly wanted back, with the warmth the jury keeps daring. All three share: a 2-D verlet/PBD elastic membrane, multi-touch grab/flick, **continuous `setTargetAtTime` pitch-bend** of a sustained just-intonation chord over A2/110Hz (NO note-tapping anywhere), kids-safe `gainв†’lowpassв‰¤8kв†’compressorв†’destination` limiter, alive-from-frame-one shimmer + a silent idle auto-demo so the 06:30 glance sings with zero setup. Winner shipped = `579-silk-choir` (WebGPU compute solver + Canvas2D fallback + runtime hot-downgrade; sustained grab-stretch bends the chord up to ~5 semitones + brightening). Floor: honest **3/5** (#2 в‰Ґ3 subsystems + #3 Jakobsen verlet PBD / Ondes-Martenot-Theremin continuous-pitch lineage; #1 NOT claimed вЂ” verlet exists at 303 as 1-D strings; #5 NOT claimed вЂ” no <14-day bind).

### 580-silk-veil вЂ” `queued` (banked DEEP non-winner, cycle 414 В· multi-touch grab-stretch В· **Canvas2D** silk В· kids / warm-tactile) вЂ” the bulletproof-iPad path
**Same concept as 579 (grab and pull a silk sheet; tension bends a continuous warm chord), rendered entirely in Canvas2D** вЂ” a CPU verlet solver (32Г—22 grid, 4 relaxation iterations) drawn as glowing translucent silk (additive gradient quad fills warming with stretch, warp/weft filament lines, a drifting specular highlight, grab halos), held to 60fps on a mid iPad; six column-regions each a voice of a JI major-add9 over A2, pitch gliding ~4 semitones with stretch + lowpass opening, via `setTargetAtTime` portamento. **Why it didn't win (cycle 414):** the **most reliable on every device** and a genuinely beautiful, warm, physical-feeling drape вЂ” but it is **Canvas2D-only, so it does NOT revive the jury-starved WebGPU** (the jury's explicit ask this cycle), whereas 579/581 run WebGPU *when available* AND fall back to Canvas2D, making them strictly better on that axis. **Resurrect** when the cycle's priority is maximum iPad reliability / the lowest-end-device path, or to ship as 579's more-portable sibling; it is the most bulletproof of the three. Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `membrane.ts`, `audio.ts`, `render.ts`, `README.md`.

### 581-silk-ripple вЂ” `queued` (banked DEEP non-winner, cycle 414 В· touch FLICK/slap в†’ traveling waves В· **WebGPU** + Canvas2D В· kids / playful-splashy) вЂ” the dynamic-gesture variant
**Same membrane, different interaction: flick or slap the sheet and an impulse propagates as visible traveling WAVES that roll across the silk and reflect off the pinned edges over ~2s; as each crest rolls through a vertical band, that band's voice pitch + brightness glide up and back continuously with the local wave amplitude вЂ” so a flick sends an audible *bend* rippling through a 7-voice JI chord.** WebGPU compute solver (ping-pong displacement buffers, additive point-cloud render) + CPU/Canvas2D fallback. **Why it didn't win (cycle 414):** the **most immediately fun for a 4yo** (slap it, watch waves splash, hear the chord ripple) and it also revives WebGPU вЂ” but (a) it is a *variant* of the headline concept rather than the headline itself (the brief's core is "grab and PULL," which 579 IS), and (b) its bend is subtler (~2.2 semitones vs 579's ~5), so the continuous-pitch break from the pentatonic-tap is less pronounced and it reads slightly less warm/expressive at a silent glance. **Resurrect** for a playful/percussive kids fire, or fold its wave-propagation into 579 as a "flick to send a ripple through the held chord" gesture (the clean cycle-2 deepening вЂ” sustained-pull AND flick-ripple in one sheet). Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `membrane.ts`, `gpu.ts`, `audio.ts`, `render.ts`, `README.md`.

## В§416 вЂ” banked from the cycle 416 KIDS DEEP fire (whole-body camera instrument)

Two non-winners from the 416 "dance and the room sings" DEEP fire. Both are built, demoable, and were `rm -rf`'d after curating `582-kids-dance-sky` вЂ” resurrect from these specs (re-allocate fresh numbers).

### `kids-shadow-band` (built as 581, banked) вЂ” status: `queued`
Pure **Canvas2D frame-differencing** whole-body instrument, **zero deps, bulletproof on any iPad** (no model download, instant). Front camera в†’ 160Г—120 offscreen diff в†’ motion painted as warm additively-glowing colored light-trails (~0.5s fade) over a dark calm room вЂ” never a mirror photo. 6 vertical zones, each a warm voice; *where* you move picks the voice, *how much* drives loudness/brightness, stillness settles to a root+fifth JI-Lydian drone bed. Krueger *Videoplace* / Daniel Rozin "body as light." **Resurrect when:** MediaPipe pose proves flaky on Karel's real iPad (this is the no-download fallback path), OR as an adult-mode bulletproof Videoplace. Was a hair closer to the spatial-grid reflex than 582's semantic body mapping вЂ” the only reason it lost.

### `kids-light-ribbons` (built as 583, banked) вЂ” status: `queued`
**Canvas2D dense optical-flow** (16Г—12 grid, one-iteration Lucas-Kanade) в†’ a **continuous body-bowed warm choir**: speed+upward motion glide the 5 voices up a JI-Lydian scale (log-space portamento via `setTargetAtTime`, never a clicked note), speed opens the lowpass, horizontal direction tilts the voicing; stillness в†’ root+fifth+octave drone. Warm particles advected along the flow leave glowing ribbons. Ondes Martenot/Theremin continuous-pitch lineage + Krueger. Tension you **feel**, not solve вЂ” exactly the jury ask. **Resurrect when:** `579-silk-choir` (the other continuous-bent-warm-choir) is out of the last-10 diversity window вЂ” it lost THIS cycle only on adjacency to 579, not on quality. The freshest *musical* idea of the three.

### Banked В§417 (cycle 417 ADULT DEEP non-winners вЂ” TEXT seeds, folders removed; renumber on revival, max folder now 583):
Both extend the jury-blessed + Karel-loved "his real piano as the seed, warm not puzzle" lineage; both lost ONLY on diversity-overlap with existing loved clusters, not on quality. Each is built-and-proven (lint/type-clean) and can be resurrected fast.

- **`584-piano-spectral-tide`** (phase-vocoder spectral FREEZE) вЂ” `queued`. Load + STFT Karel's real piano (fftSize 2048, 75% overlap, magnitude+phase per frame); drag a playhead along his timeline and wherever you pause the spectral frame **freezes** into a sustained, infinitely-held warm drone (additive bank of the top-48 magnitude bins as continuously-phased sine oscillators вЂ” no metallic frozen-FFT buzz); slow drag = a continuous time-stretched legato scrub through his harmonies; a vertical **depth** axis crossfades crisp-frozen в†” lowpassed-veil. WebGL2 fragment-shader **spectral tide** (1-D spectrum texture в†’ drifting warm indigoв†’violetв†’amberв†’rose strata + playhead light), Canvas2D fallback, idle auto-self-scrub. Refs: Flanagan & Golden (1966) / Mark Dolson "The Phase Vocoder: A Tutorial" (1986); Г‰liane Radigue / William Basinski *Disintegration Loops*. **Promising:** the warmest, most oceanic of the three; a true "stop time inside his chord" piece; nods his loved ocean/aurora cluster (107вќ¤пёЏ/262вќ¤пёЏ). **Caveat that lost it THIS cycle:** spectral-freeze/spectral-cloud overlaps his already-loved spectral cluster (`243-spectral-cloud`вќ¤пёЏ, `267-spectral-drift`вќ¤пёЏ, `321-spectral-flight`вќ¤пёЏ) вЂ” too close to ship in the same window. **Resurrect** once that cluster is out of the 10-window, or fold in as a "freeze lens" on 583's corpus. Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `audio.ts` (STFT), `vocoder.ts`, `gl.ts`, `README.md`.

- **`585-piano-grain-orrery`** (n-body physics в†’ granular retrigger) вЂ” `queued`. Slice his piano into ~130 grains (each remembering source offset + brightness + RMS); each becomes a luminous **body orbiting a soft central attractor** in a 2-D gravity field (central pull + short-range repulsion). **Stir** with pointer/touch вЂ” a moving gravity well + a swirl impulse from drag velocity perturbs the orbits; a body **voices** its grain (panned by x, filtered by velocity/radius) when it swings near the core, the cursor, or crosses an outward sounding-ring. The music is the **emergent chorus** of his grains orbiting вЂ” dense while you stir, sparse and meditative when it settles (в‰¤16 simultaneous voices, limiter). WebGL2 additive point-sprites with ping-pong feedback-texture motion trails; Canvas2D fallback; idle auto-demo. Refs: Curtis Roads *Microsound* / Xenakis grain-clouds; Ventrella/Mohr *Particle Life*; music-of-the-spheres orrery framing. **Promising:** the richest *visual* of the three (852-line render), the most "alive while idle," cosmic-but-intimate. **Caveat that lost it THIS cycle:** physicsв†’granular is lovely but particle/n-body systems are heavily represented in the lab (`130-tsl-particle-compute`вќ¤пёЏ, `236-particle-life-song`вќ¤пёЏ, `262-aurora-particle`вќ¤пёЏ) and "physicsв†’retrigger" is less of a lab-first than 583's target-matched concatenation. **Resurrect** for a physics-forward fire, or as 583's "orrery lens." Built files (removed): `page.tsx`, `audio.ts`, `physics.ts`, `README.md`.
